# Pudd’nhead Wilson — A Whisper to the Reader

### *(Paathak Ke Liye Ek Gupt Sandesh)*

---

> **TO THE READER.** *(Paathak Ke Liye)*
> *There is no character, howsoever good and fine, but it can be destroyed by ridicule, howsoever poor and witless. Observe the ass, for instance: his character is about perfect, he is the choicest spirit among all the humbler animals, yet see what ridicule has brought him to. Instead of feeling complimented when we are called an ass, we are left in doubt.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Aisa koi charitra [character] nahi hai, chahe woh kitna bhi achha aur umda kyun na ho, jise mazaak aur uphaas [ridicule] ke zariye tabaah na kiya ja sake, chahe woh mazaak kitna bhi ghatiya aur moorkhta-purna [witless] kyun na ho. Udaharan ke liye, gadhe [ass] ko dekhein: uska charitra lagbhag perfect hai, woh saare vinamra jaanwaaron mein sabse behad shreshth aatma hai, phir bhi dekho mazaak ne uski kya haalat kar di hai. Jab hamein koi gadha kehta hai, toh tareef mehsoos karne ke bajaye, hum shak mein pad jaate hain.)*

---

Ek aisa insaan jo kanooni mamlon (legal matters) se anjaan hai, usse hamesha galtiyan hone ki sambhavna rehti hai jab woh apne pen se kisi court ke scene ko portrait karne (photograph) ki koshish karta hai; aur isliye main is kitab mein kanoon ke chapters ko pehle ek trained barrister—agar unhein yahi kaha jata hai—dwara kade aur thaka dene wale vishleshan (rigid and exhausting revision) aur correction ke bina press mein bhejne ke liye taiyar nahi tha. Yeh chapters ab har ek detail mein sahi hain, kyunki unhein William Hicks ki seedhi nazar ke tehat dobara likha gaya hai, jinhone thirty-five saal pehle southwest Missouri mein kuch samay ke liye kanoon adhyayan kiya tha aur phir apni health ke liye yahan Florence aa gaye the aur abhi bhi Piazza del Duomo se kona ghoomte hi piche ki gali mein majood Macaroni Vermicelli ke ghode-ke-chare wale shed (horse-feed shed) mein exercise aur khane-peene ke badle madad kar rahe hain. Yeh theek us ghar ke thoda pare hai jahan woh patthar jisme Dante cheh sau saal pehle baitha karte the wall mein lagaya gya hai, jab woh aisa dikhava karte (let on) the ki woh unhein Giotto’s campanile (ghanta-ghar) banate hue dekh rahe hain aur phir bhi jaise hi Beatrice apna bachaav karne ke liye chestnut cake ka ek tukda lene ke raaste se guzarti thin (is darr se ki kahin school pahunche se pehle Ghibelline ka vidroh [outbreak] na ho jaye) toh woh dekhkar turant thak jaate the, usi purane stand par jahan woh aaj bhi wahi purani cake bechte hain aur yeh aaj bhi utni hi halki aur achhi hai jitni tab thi, aur yeh koi tareef (flattery) nahi hai, isse bahut door hai. Kanoon par unka haath thoda tang tha (He was a little rusty), lekin unhone is kitab ke liye abhyas kiya (rubbed up), aur woh do ya teen kanooni chapters ab poori tarah sahi aur seedhe hain. Unhone mujhe khud aisa bataya tha.

2 January, 1893 ko mere haathon dwara, Florence se teen miles piche, pahadiyon par sthit Settignano village ke Villa Viviani mein diya gaya—yeh jagah nishchit roop se is planet par majood sabse aakarshak nazaara (most charming view) pradan karti hai, aur iske sath hi kisi bhi planet ya yahan tak ki kisi bhi solar system mein dhoondhe jaane wale sabse khayali aur jaadui sunset (dreamlike and enchanting sunsets) pradan karti hai—aur ghar ke sabse shandaar room (swell room) mein diya gaya, jahan Cerretani senators aur is vansh ke doosre bade amiron (grandees) ke busts (aadhe sharir ki moortiyan) mujh par swikriti se neeche dekh rahi hain, jaise woh Dante par dekha karti thin, aur shaanti se mujhse pooch rahi hain ki main unhein apni family mein apna loon, jise main khushi ke sath karta hoon, kyunki mere sabse door ke poorvaj (remotest ancestors) in robed aur stately antiques ke samne abhi-abhi nikle nau-sikhia bache (spring chickens) jaise hain, aur yeh mere liye ek badi aur santoshjanak badhottari (satisfying lift) hogi, woh cheh sau saal ki badhottari hogi.

— Mark Twain

---

# Chapter I — Pudd’nhead Wins His Name

### *(Pudd’nhead Ko Uska Naam Milta Hai)*

---

> *Tell the truth or trump—but get the trick.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Sach bolo ya turup ka ikka chalo—lekin chal [trick] haasil karo.)*

---

Is vritant (chronicle) ka scene Mississippi ke Missouri side par sthit Dawson’s Landing naam ka town hai, jo St. Louis se steamboat ke zariye aadhe din ki yatra ki doori par hai.

1830 mein yeh mamuli ek- aur do-manzil ke lakdi ke makanon (frame dwellings) ka ek chhota sa sahuliyat-bhara sangrah (snug collection) tha jinki whitewashed (choone se poti hui) baahri deewarein lagbhag gulab ki belon, honeysuckles aur morning-glories ke aapas mein uljhe ghaatank dhero (tangles) se nazar se chhupi hui thin. Inme se har ek khoobsurat ghar ke samne safed lakdi ke dondon (white palings) se ghira ek garden tha jo gulkhaire (hollyhocks), marigolds, touch-me-nots, prince’s-feathers aur doosre purane fashion ke phoolon se bhabhaka (opulently stocked) raha tha; jabki makanon ki khidkiyon ki dehleez (window-sills) par lakdi ke boxes rakkhe the jinmein moss-rose ke plants the aur terra-cotta (mitti) ke pots the jinmein geranium ki ek aishi prajati ugti thi jiske tivra laal rang ke phoolon ka phailav gulab se dhake ghar ke samne ke hisse ke halkay pink rang ko aag ke dhamake (explosion of flame) ki tarah highlight (accented) karta tha. Jab pots aur boxes ke baahar dehleez (ledge) par kisi cat ke liye jagah hoti thi, toh sunny weather mein cat wahan hoti thi—poori lambai mein phhaili hui, sooriyan aur anandit (blissful), sooraj ki taraf apni baal-daar belly (furry belly) kiye aur naak ke upar ek paw curve kiye hue. Tab woh ghar poora hota tha, aur iska santoosh aur shanti is symbol dwara duniya ke samne zahir (made manifest) hoti thi, jiski gavaahi bilkul achook (infallible) hai. Ek ghar bina kisi cat ke—aur ek achhi tarah se khilayi-pilayi, dulaari (well-petted) aur properly sammanit (revered) cat ke bina—shayad ek perfect ghar ho sakta hai, lekin woh apna adhikaar-patra (title) kaise prove kar sakta hai?

Poori sarkon ke sath, dono sides par, eent ke sidewalks (sidewalks) ke baahri edge par, locust ke trees khade the jinke tana (trunks) lakdi ke boxing se protected the, aur yeh sardi mein chhaon aur spring mein ek meethi fragrance (khushbu) pradan karte the jab kalyon ke guchhe (clusters of buds) baahar aate the. Mukhya sarak, jo river se ek block peeche aur uske parallel chalti thi, akeli business sarak thi. Yeh cheh blocks lambi thi, aur har block mein teen manzil oonchi eent ki do ya teen stores, beech-beech mein majood (interjected) choti lakdi ki shops ke dhero ke upar oonchi uthi thin. Latakte hue swinging signs poori sarak ki lambai mein hawa mein creak (ch चरमराते) the. Woh candy-striped (patti-daar) danda jo Venice ke mahalon se ghire canals ke sath ek garv-bhare aur ancient roop se kulinata (nobility) ko sanket deta hai, Dawson’s Landing ki mukhya sarak ke sath kevel ek mamuli barber shop ko sanket deta tha. Ek mukhya kone par ek ooncha bina paint kiya danda khada tha jo top se bottom tak tin ke pots, pans aur cups se ghira (wreathed) tha, jo mukhya tinmonger (tin ke bartan bechne wale) ka duniya ke samne (jab hawa chalti thi) ek shor-bhara notice tha ki us kone par business ke liye uski shop majood hai.

Is hamlet (chhhote gaon) ka samne ka hissa badi river ke saaf pani se dhota tha; iska sharir peeche ki taraf ek halke dhalan (gentle incline) par phhaila tha; iska sabse piche ka border badhte hue pahadiyon ke base-line par apne gharon ko bikhair (scattered) deta tha; pahadiyan oonchi uthi thin, town ko ek half-moon curve (ardh-chandrakaar ghumaav) mein ghere hue, jo pair se lekar peak tak jangaloon se dhaki (clothed) thin.

Steamboats har ek ghante mein aage-peeche guzarti thin. Choti Cairo line aur choti Memphis line se talluk rakhne wali steamboats hamesha rukti thin; bade Orleans liners sirf ishara karne (hails) par, ya passengers ya maal (freight) utarne ke liye rukte the; aur yahi haal “transients” (kabhi-kabar aane-jaane wale) ke vishal bedon (flotilla) ke sath bhi tha. Yeh baad wale doze bhashon ki rivers se aate the—Illinois, Missouri, Upper Mississippi, Ohio, Monongahela, Tennessee, Red River, White River, aur isi tarah aage bhi; aur har taraf jaane ke liye taiyar the aur har us dimaag mein aane suvidha (comfort) ya zarurat ke saaman se bhare (stocked) the jise Mississippi ki communities chaah sakti thin, Falls of St. Anthony ke barfeele hisse se lekar nau climates ke zariye garm New Orleans tak.

Dawson’s Landing ek gulam rakhne wala (slaveholding) town tha, jiske peeche gulamon dwara joti jaane wali grain aur pork ki ek ameer country thi. Town sleepy (susta), comfortable aur santusht tha. Yeh fifty saal purana tha, aur slowly badh raha tha—actually bahut slowly, lekin phir bhi yeh badh raha tha.

Mukhya citizen York Leicester Driscoll the, lagbhag forty saal ke, county court ke judge. Unhein apne purane Virginian poorvajon (ancestry) par bahut garv tha, aur apni mehmaan-nawazi (hospitalities) aur apne kaafi formal aur shandaar tareeqon (stately manners) mein woh unqi traditions ko barkarar rakhte the. Woh umda, nyay-priya aur udaar (generous) the. Ek gentleman banna—bina kisi daag ya dhabbe (stain or blemish) ke gentleman banna—unka akela religion tha, aur iske prati woh hamesha faithful the. Poori community dwara unki respect, izzat (esteemed) aur pyaar kiya jata tha. Woh acche khase ameer (well off) the, aur gradually apne bhandar ko badha rahe the. Woh aur unki wife lagbhag happy the, lekin poori tarah nahi, kyunki unke koi bache nahi the. Ek bachhe ke khazane ke liye tivra ichha (longing) saalon ke phisalne ke sath-sath stronger aur stronger hoti gayi thin, lekin woh blessing kabhi nahi aayi—aur kabhi nahi aane wali thi.

Is couple ke sath Judge ki vidhwa sister, Mrs. Rachel Pratt rehti thin, aur woh bhi childless thin—childless, aur us kaaran se udaas (sorrowful), aur santusht na hone wali (not to be comforted). Woh auraten achhi aur sadharan (commonplace) log thin, aur apni duty karti thin aur unhein saaf zameer (clear consciences) aur community ki sahamati (approbation) mein apna reward milta tha. Woh Presbyterians thin, Judge ek free-thinker (swatantra-vicharak) the.

Pembroke Howard, lawyer aur bachelor, umra lagbhag forty, ek aur purane Virginian amir (grandee) the jinke poorvaj First Families se prooved the. Woh ek umda, brave, aur prabhavshali prani (majestic creature) the, Virginia rule ke sabse baareek manandando (nicest requirements) ke mutabik ek gentleman, ek samarpit Presbyterian, “code” (maryada-kanoon) par ek authority, aur ek aishi insaan jo hamesha shishtata se (courteously) field mein aapke samne khade hone ke liye taiyar rehte the agar unka koi act ya word aapko shak-bhara lagta, aur aapke pasand ke kisi bhi hathiyar ke sath—brad-awls se lekar topkhana (artillery) tak—use explain karne ke liye taiyar rehte. Woh logon ke beech bahut popular the, aur Judge ke sabse kareebi dost the.

Phir Colonel Cecil Burleigh Essex the, ek aur bade caliber ke F. F. V. (First Families of Virginia)—halanki, unse hamara koi talluk nahi hai.

Percy Northumberland Driscoll, Judge ke bhai, aur unse paanch saal chote, ek married mard the, aur unke hearthstone (bhatthi/aangan) ke chaaron taraf bache rahe the; lekin unpar ek-ek karke measles, croup aur scarlet fever ne hamla kiya, aur isne doctor ko apne effective purane zamane ke tareeqon (antediluvian methods) ka use karne ka ek chance diya; isliye palne (cradles) khaali the. Woh ek kamyab (prosperous) mard the, speculations (satte-baazi/vyapar) ke liye ek achha head rakhne wale, aur unqi fortune badh rahi thi. 1 February, 1830 ko unke ghar do boy babes paada hue: ek unke yahan, doosra unqi gulam ladkiyon mein se ek ke yahan, jiska naam Roxana tha. Roxana twenty saal ki thin. Woh usi din uth kar chaaron taraf ghoom rahi thin, haath poori tarah se bhare (hands full) hone ke sath, kyunki woh dono babies ko sambhal (tending) rahi thin.

Mrs. Percy Driscoll ek hafte ke andar mar gayin. Roxy bacchon ke charge mein rahi. Unka apna tareeqa chalta tha, kyunki Mr. Driscoll jald hi speculations mein absorbed (leeng) ho gaye aur unhein unke apne hi upaayon (devices) par chhod diya.

Usi February ke mahine mein, Dawson’s Landing ko ek naya citizen mila. Yeh Mr. David Wilson the, Scotch parentage (poorvajon) ke ek young bande. Woh apna bhagya (fortune) dhoondhne ke liye New York State ke andaruni hisse mein sthit apne birthplace se is door-daas ke kshetra (remote region) mein bhatak (wandered) aaye the. Woh twenty-five saal ke the, college-bred (padhe-likhe) the, aur unhone ek doosre saal pehle ek Eastern law school mein post-college course khatam kiya tha.

Woh ek sadharan dikhne wale (homely), freckled (jhaiyon-waale), sandy-haired young bande the, ek intelligent blue eye ke sath jisme saaf-safai (frankness) aur saathi-pan (comradeship) tha aur ek pleasant tarah ki chhupi hui chamak (covert twinkle) thi. Agar unki ek badkismat tippani (unfortunate remark) na hoti, toh woh bina kisi shakk ke Dawson’s Landing mein turant ek safal career mein enter kar gaye hote. Lekin unhone village mein bitaye apne pehle hi din apna fatal remark (ghaatank tippani) kiya, aur isne unhein naap (gaged) diya. Unki abhi-abhi citizens ke ek group se mulaqat hui thi jab ek invisible (jo dikh nahi raha tha) dog ne yelp (bhaunkna), snarl (ghurrana) aur howl (rona) shuru kar diya aur apne aap ko poori tarah se na-pasand (disagreeable) bana diya, jispar young Wilson ne kuch aisa kaha, jaise koi zor se soch raha ho—

“Kaash main us dog ke aadhe hisse ka malik (owned half) hota.”

“Kyun?” kisi ne poocha.

“Kyunki main apne aadhe hisse ko maar deta.”

Group ne jigyasa ke sath, yahan tak ki chinta ke sath unke face ko dhoondha (searched), lekin wahan koi roshni nahi mili, koi aisa expression nahi jise woh padh sakein. Woh unse aise peeche hat gaye (fell away) jaise kisi ajeeb/paralaukik (uncanny) cheez se hte hain, aur unpar discuss karne ke liye akele mein (privacy) chale gaye. Ek ne kaha:

“Lagta hai (Pears) ki bewakoof hai.”

“Lagta hai?” doosre ne kaha. “Hai, main sochta hoon aap behtar kahein.”

“Kaha ki kaash woh dog ke aadhe hisse ka malik hota, idiot,” teesre ne kaha. “Usne kya socha ki agle aadhe hisse ka kya hoga agar usne apneaadhe hisse ko maar diya? Kya aap assume karte hain ki usne socha woh zinda rahega?”

“Kyun, usne nishchit roop se aisa socha hoga, jab tak ki woh duniya ka sabse downrightest (poora) bewakoof na ho; kyunki agar usne aisa na socha hota, toh woh poore dog ka malik banna chahta, yeh jaante hue ki agar usne apne aadhe hisse ko maar diya aur agla aadha hissa mar gaya, toh woh us aadhe hisse ke liye bhi waisa hi responsible (zimmedar) hoga jaise ki usne apne bajaye us aadhe hisse ko maara ho. Kya yeh aapko is tareeqe se nahi dikhta, gents?”

“Haan, aisa hi hai. Agar woh samanya dog (general dog) ke ek aadhe hisse ka malik hota, toh aisa hota; agar woh dog ke ek end ka malik hota aur doosra insaan doosre end ka malik hota, toh waisa hi hota, theek same; khhasakar pehle case mein, kyunki agar aap ek general dog ke ek aadhe hisse ko maar dete hain, toh koi aisa mard nahi hai jo bata sake ki woh kiska aadha hissa tha, lekin agar woh dog ke ek end ka malik hota, toh shayad woh uske apne end ko maar sakta aur—”

“Nahi, woh aisa bhi nahi kar sakta tha; woh aisa nahi kar sakta tha aur responsible na ho agar doosra end mar jata, jo ki woh marta. Meri raai mein mard apne sahi dimaag (right mind) mein nahi hai.”

“Meri raai mein uske paas koi dimaag hi nahi hai.”

No. 3 ne kaha: “Well, woh ek lummox (anadi/mota) hai, anyway.”

“Wahi toh woh hai,” No. 4 ne kaha, “woh ek labrick (murkh) hai—bas ek Simon-pure labrick (asli murkh) hai, agar kabhi koi tha.”

“Haan, sir, woh ek dam fool (mahaji-murkh) hai, is tareeqe se main use rakhta hoon,” No. 5 ne kaha. “Koi bhi jo chahta hai different soch sakta hai, lekin yeh mere vichaar (sentiments) hain.”

“Main aapke sath hoon, gentlemen,” No. 6 ne kaha. “Perfect jackass (gadha)—haanh, aur yeh kehna bahut aage nahi ja raha hai ki woh ek **pudd’nhead (gadha/murkh)** hai. Agar woh pudd’nhead nahi hai, toh main koi judge nahi hoon, bas itna hi.”

Mr. Wilson chune gaye the. Yeh incident poore town mein bataya gya, aur har kisi dwara gombhirta se discuss (gravely discussed) kiya gya. Ek hafte ke andar unhone apna pehla naam kho diya; *Pudd’nhead* ne iski jagah le li. Samay ke sath unhein pasand kiya jaane laga, aur kaafi achhi tarah pasand bhi kiya gya; lekin us samay tak nickname achhi tarah se chipak gya tha, aur yeh tik gaya. Us pehle din ke faisale (verdict) ne unhein ek bewakoof bana diya, aur woh ise kharij (set aside) karwane, ya thoda badalwane (modified) mein bhi kabil nahi rahe. Nickname ne jald hi apne sath kisi bhi karrwi ya gair-dostana bhavna (harsh or unfriendly feeling) ko carry karna band kar diya, lekin isne apni jagah banaye rakkhi, aur twenty lambe saalon tak apni jagah barkarar rakhne wala tha.

---

## The 9 Principles Checklist of Ultralearning

*(Ultralearning Ke 9 Niyamon Ki Printable Checklist)*

Aapke naye adhyayan prayason (learning projects) ke liye, Pudd’nhead Wilson ki tarah galat faisaloon se bachne aur sateekta se aage badhne ke liye yeh ranniti checklist (Checklist) hamesha kaam aayegi:

* **[ ] 1. Metalearning (Pehle Ek Map Banayein):** Adhyayan shuru karne se pehle kul expected samay ka 10% research par lagayein (Why, What, aur How ka hisab nikaalein).
* **[ ] 2. Focus (Apni Chhaku Ko Tez Karein):** Kaam ko talne (procrastination) aur bhatkaav (distraction) ke sroton ko mitaein. 5-minute rule ya Pomodoro ka use karein.
* **[ ] 3. Directness (Seedhe Aage Badhein):** Usi environment ya context mein karke seekhein (learning by doing) jahan skill ko actually apply karna hai.
* **[ ] 4. Drill (Apne Sabse Kamzor Point Par Hamla Karein):** Rate-determining step ko isolate karein aur complex skill ke chote hisson par alag se maharat haasil karein.
* **[ ] 5. Retrieval (Seekhne Ke Liye Test Karein):** Kitab band karke memory se active recall karein. Desirable difficulties ka fayda uthaein.
* **[ ] 6. Feedback (Punches Se Mat Bacho):** Harsh aur honest feedback se signal nikaalein aur noise ko ignore karein. Ego ko beech mein na laein.
* **[ ] 7. Retention (Ek Tooti Hui Balti Ko Mat Bharo):** Spaced-repetition software (SRS) ka use karein, core skills ko proceduralize aur overlearning karein.
* **[ ] 8. Intuition (Upar Build Karne Se Pehle Gehra Khodein):** Gaps ko dhoondhne ke liye Feynman Technique ka use karein aur concrete examples se shuru karein.
* **[ ] 9. Experimentation (Apni Aaram-dayak Seema Se Baahar Explore Karein):** Resources, techniques aur styles ke sath prayog karke extremes ko explore karein.

---

# Chapter II — Driscoll Spares His Slaves

### *(Driscoll Apne Gulamon Ko Baksh Deta Hai)*

---

> *Adam was but human—this explains it all. He did not want the apple for the apple’s sake, he wanted it only because it was forbidden. The mistake was in not forbidding the serpent; then he would have eaten the serpent.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Adam bhi aakhirkar ek insaan hi the—yeh sab kuch explain kar deta hai. Woh seb ko seb ke lalach mein nahi chahte the, woh ise sirf isliye chahte the kyunki iski manahi [forbidden] thi. Galti saanp ko mana na karne mein thi; agar aisa kiya hota, toh woh saanp ko hi kha gaye hote.)*

---

Pudd’nhead Wilson ke paas aane par thode se paise (trifle of money) the, aur unhone town ke bilkul western edge (verge) par ek chhota sa ghar kharid liya. Uske aur Judge Driscoll ke ghar ke beech sirf ek ghaas ka aangan (grassy yard) tha, jiske beech mein ek paling fence (lakdi ka donda) dono properties ko divide karta tha. Unhone town mein ek chhota sa office rent par liya aur ek tin ka sign bahar taang diya, jis par yeh sabd likhe the:

**DAVID WILSON.**

**ATTORNEY AND COUNSELOR-AT-LAW.**

**SURVEYING, CONVEYANCING, ETC.**

Lekin unqi us ghaatank tippani (deadly remark) ne unka chance barbaad kar diya tha—kam se kam kanoon (law) ke kshetra mein toh bilkul. Koi bhi clients nahi aaye. Kuch samay baad, unhone apna sign board neeche utara, aur kanoon wale features ko mita kar (knocked out) ise apne ghar par taang diya. Ab yeh ek jameen-maapak (land-surveyor) aur expert accountant ke roop mein unqi mamuli kshamtayon (humble capacities) ki services offer kar raha tha. Kabhi-kabar unhein surveying ka koi kaam mil jata, aur kabhi-kabar koi merchant apne khata-bahi ko theek karne (straighten out his books) ke liye unhein bula leta. Scotch sabr (patience) aur sahas (pluck) ke sath unhone apni is kharab reputation ke sath jeene aur kanooni kshetra mein apna rasta banane ka nishchay kiya. Bechaare bande, woh pehle se nahi dekh sakte (foresee) the ki aisa karne mein unhein kitna thaka dene wala lamba samay (weary long time) lagne wala tha.

Unke paas bekar samay (idle time) ka ek vishal bhandar tha, lekin yeh unke haathon par kabhi bhaari nahi laga, kyunki unhone ideas ke brahmand mein paada hone wali har ek nayi cheez mein interest liya, aur apne ghar par iska adhyayan (studied) aur ispar prayog (experimented) kiya. Unke pasandida dhunon (pet fads) mein se ek hastarekha-vigyan (palmistry) tha. Ek doosre fad ko unhone koi naam nahi diya tha, aur na hi woh kisi ke samne explain karte the ki iska maqsad kya tha, balki simply kehte the ki yeh ek manoranjan (amusement) hai. In fact, unhone paaya tha ki unke ye fads unhein ek pudd’nhead ke roop mein mazeed badhava dete hain; isliye woh unke baare mein zyaada baatcheet karne (communicative) se parhez karne lage the.

Bina naam wala woh fad logon ke finger-marks (ungliyon ke nishaan) se deal karta tha. Woh apni coat ki pocket mein ek halki box carry karte the jisme grooves (khhache) bane the, aur un grooves mein five inches lambi aur three inches choudi glass ki strips thin. Har strip ke neeche ke edge par safed paper ki ek patti pasted thi. Woh logon se apne haathon ko apne baalon mein pherne ke liye kehte (is tarah unpar natural oil ki ek thin coating ikhatha ho jaati) aur phir glass strip par ek thumb-mark banane ke liye kehte, jiske baad ek-ek karke har ungli ke gole ka nishaan (ball of each finger) nikaalte. In dhundhle chiknai ke nishaanon (grease-prints) ki row ke neeche woh safed paper ki patti par record likhte—is tareeqe se:

*JOHN SMITH, right hand—*

aur mahine ka din aur saal add karte, phir ek doosri glass strip par Smith ka left hand lete, aur naam, date aur "left hand" sabd add karte. Strips ko ab wapas grooved box mein rakh diya jata, aur unhone unhein un cheezon ke beech jagah di jise Wilson apne "records" kehte the.

Woh aksar apne records ka study karte, badi dilchasp (absorbing interest) ke sath der raat tak unhein jaanchte aur unmein doobe rehte; lekin unhein wahan kya mila—agar unhein kuch mila bhi—woh kisi ke samne zahir (revealed) nahi karte the. Kabhi-kabhi woh kisi ungli ke gole dwara chhode gaye jatil aur naazuk dhaanche (involved and delicate pattern) ko paper par copy karte, aur phir ek pantograph ke zariye ise vishal roop se bada (enlarged) karte taaki woh iski ghoomti hui lines ke jaal (web of curving lines) ko aasaani aur suvidha se jaanch sakein.

Ek behad garm dhoop bhari dopahar (sweltering afternoon)—woh July 1830 ka pehla din tha—woh apne kaam ke room mein uljhi hui khata-kitabhon (tangled account-books) ke ek set par kaam kar rahe the, jo westward ek khaali jameen ke dher (vacant lots) ki taraf khultaa tha, tabhi baahir ki ek baatcheet ne unhein disturb kiya. Yeh chillane (yells) ke zariye chal rahi thi, jo pradarshit karta tha ki isme engaged log ek doosre ke paas nahi the:

"Arre, Roxy, tumhara baby kaisa hai?" Yeh door ki awaaz se aaya.

"First-rate (behad achha); tum kaise ho, Jasper?" Yeh chillaahat bilkul paas se thi.

"Oh, main thik-thak (middlin') hoon; shikayat karne ke liye kuch nahi hai. Main jaldi hi tumse ishq ladane (a-court'n') aane wala hoon, Roxy."

"Tum aane wale ho, tum black mud-cat (gande paani ki machhli)! Yah—yah—yah! Mere paas tum jaise black niggers ke sath socializing ke mukable kuch mazeed behtar karne ke liye hai. Kya ole Miss Cooper ki Nancy ne tumhein nikaal diya (give you the mitten) hai?" Roxy ne is vyang (sally) ke sath bina-chinta wali hansi (care-free laughter) chhodi.

"Aap jealous hain, Roxy, aapke sath yahi mamla hai, aap hussy (chalak)—yah—yah—yah! Is baar maine aapko pakad (got you) liya!"

"Oh, haan, tumne mujhe pakad liya, hai na. Sach keh rahi hoon Jasper, agar yeh tumhara ghamand tumhare dimaag mein ghus gya (strikes in), toh yeh tumhein nishchit roop se maar dega. Agar tum mere hote toh main tumhein bahut door jaane se pehle hi river ke neeche (sell down the river) bech deti. Pehli baar jab main tumhare master se takraungi, main unhein aisa kehne ja rahi hoon."

Yeh bekar aur bina maqsad ki baatcheet (idle and aimless jabber) lagaatar chalti rahi, dono parties is dostana dwandv (friendly duel) ka anand le rahi thin aur har ek exchanged kiye gaye is vyang-baani (wit) ke apne hisse se santusht tha—kyunki woh ise wit hi maante the.

Wilson bhashan ke prati-dvandviyon (combatants) ko dekhne ke liye khidki ke paas aaye; jab tak unqi yeh baatcheet jaatri rehti woh kaam nahi kar sakte the. Wahan khaali jameen par Jasper tha, young, koyle jaisa black (coal-black) aur ek shandaar kad-kaathi (magnificent build) wala, karrwi dhoop (pelting sun) mein ek kachre-gaadi (wheelbarrow) par baitha hua—supposably kaam par, jabki actually woh shuru karne se pehle ek ghante ka aaram karke iske liye khud ko prepare hi kar raha tha. Wilson ke porch ke samne Roxy khadi thin, haath se bani ek local bacchon wali wagon ke sath, jisme unke dono charges (bache) baithe the—ek-ek end par aur ek doosre ki taraf face kiye hue. Roxy ke bolne ke tareeqe se, koi stranger expect karta ki woh black hongi, lekin woh nahi thin. Unka sirf ek-solahva (one sixteenth) hissa black tha, aur woh ek-solahva hissa dikhta nahi tha. Woh ek prabhavshali form aur stature (kad-kaathi) ki thin, unke postures imposing aur moorti jaise (statuesque) the, aur unke gestures aur movements ek umda aur shandaar shaandari (noble and stately grace) se alag the. Unka complexion bahut fair tha, cheeks mein mazboot health ki laal chamak (rosy glow) ke sath, unka face charitra aur expression se bhara tha, unki aankhein brown aur liquid (gehri) thin, aur unke paas fine soft baalon ka ek bhaari dher tha jo brown bhi tha, lekin yeh fact saaf nahi tha kyunki unka head ek checkered (chaukhaane wale) handkerchief se bandha tha aur baal uske neeche chhupaye gaye the. Unka face shapely, intelligent aur comely—yahan tak ki beautiful tha. Unka ek aasan, independent carriage (chalne ka tareeqa) tha—jab woh apni khud ki caste ke beech hotin—aur sath hi ek ooncha aur "sassy" (teez) tareeqa bhi tha; lekin beshak safed logon (white people) ke samne woh kaafi namra aur vineet (meek and humble) thin.

Saare maqsadon ke liye Roxy kisi ki tarah hi white thin, lekin unka woh ek-solahva hissa jo black tha, usne baaki ke fifteen parts ko outvoted (haraya) kar diya aur unhein ek negro bana diya. Woh ek gulam (slave) thin, aur us roop mein bechne yogya (salable) thin. Unka bachha thirty-one parts white tha, aur woh bhi ek gulam tha, aur kanoon aur custom ke ek bhram (fiction of law) dwara ek negro tha. Uske paas apne opponent ke mukable blue aankhein aur baal the, lekin unke paas use pehchanne ka ek asadharn tareeqa kapdo ke zariye tha: kyunki white babe soft muslin aur coral necklace pehnta tha, jabki doosra kevel ek kachhe kapde ki shirt (coarse tow-linen shirt) pehnta tha jo mushkil se uske knees tak pahuncheti thi, aur koi jewelry nahi thi. White bache ka naam Thomas à Becket Driscoll tha, doosre ka naam Valet de Chambre tha: koi surname nahi—gulamon ko yeh prathmikta (privilege) nahi thi. Roxana ne us phrase ko kahin suna tha, iske umda sound ne unke kaan ko pasand kiya tha, aur chunki unhone assume kiya tha ki yeh ek naam hai, unhone ise apne darling par laad diya. Jald hi ise short karke "Chambers" kar diya gya, beshak.

Wilson Roxy ko dekh kar jaante the, aur jab wit ka duel khatam hone laga, toh woh ek-do record ikhatha karne (gather in a record) ke liye baahar aaye. Jasper ne immediately tivrata se kaam karna shuru kar diya, yeh perceive (mehsus) karte hue ki unke aaram ko dekh liya gya hai. Wilson ne bacchon ko jaanchte (inspected) hue poocha—

"Yeh kitne bade hain, Roxy?"

"Dono same age ke hain, sir—five months. Born pehli Feb’uary ko."

"Yeh handsome chote chaps hain. Ek doosre jitna hi handsome hai."

Ek khush smile ne ladki ke safed daant zahir kiye, aur unhone kaha:

"Bless yo’ soul, Misto Wilson, aapka aisa kehna pow’ful nice hai, kyunki unmein se ek sirf ek nigger hai. Mighty prime chhota nigger hai, main hamesha kehti hoon, lekin yeh is liye hai kyunki yeh mera hai, o' course."

"Aap unhein bina kapdo ke kaise pehchanti hain, Roxy?"

Roxy unqi size ke mutabik ek hansi hansin, aur unhone kaha:

"Oh, main unhein separate (pechan) sakti hoon, Misto Wilson, lekin main bet lagati hoon Marse Percy apni life bachane ke liye bhi nahi kar sakte."

Wilson ne thodi der tak baatcheet ki, aur jaldi hi unhone glass strips par Roxy ke finger-prints haasil kar liye—right hand aur left—unpar label aur date lagayi, aur dono bacchon ke "records" bhi liye, aur unpar bhi label aur date add ki.

Do mahine baad, 3 September ko, unhone finger-marks ke is trio (teenon) ko phir se liya. Unhein ek “series” (shrankhla) rakhna pasand tha, childhood ke period ke dauran intervals par do ya teen “takings”, jiske baad kai saalon ke intervals par doosre kiye jaane the.

Agle din—yaani kehna ka matlab hai, 4 September ko—kuch aisa hua jisne Roxana ko gehrai se prabhavit (profoundly impressed) kiya. Mr. Driscoll ne paise ki ek aur chhoti matra miss ki—jo yeh kehne ka ek tareeqa hai ki yeh koi nayi cheez nahi thi, balki pehle bhi ho chuki thi. In truth, yeh pehle teen baar ho chuka tha. Driscoll ka sabr khatam ho gya tha. Woh gulamon aur doosre jaanwaaron ke prati kaafi humane (dayalu) mard the; woh apni hi race ke bhatke hue (erring) logon ke prati ek tezi se humane mard the. Theft (chori) ko woh bardaasht nahi kar sakte the, aur saaf taur par unke ghar mein ek chor tha. Necessarily chor unke negroes mein se hi ek hona chahiye. Kade kadam (sharp measures) uthaye jaane chahiye. Unhone apne servants ko apne samne bulaya. Roxy ke alava wahan teen aur the: ek mard, ek aurat, aur ek twelve saal ka ladka. Unka aapas mein koi rishta nahi tha. Mr. Driscoll ne kaha:

"Aap sab ko pehle bhi warn kiya gya hai. Iska koi fayda nahi hua. Is baar main aapko ek lesson sikhaunga. Main chor ko bech dunga. Aap mein se kaun guilty (doshi) hai?"

Woh sab us threat (dhamki) par kaanp uthe (shuddered), kyunki yahan unke paas ek achha ghar tha, aur ek naya ghar badtar badlav (change for the worse) hone ki sambhavna thi. Denial samanya (general) tha. Kisi ne kuch nahi churaya tha—kam se kam paise toh nahi—thoda sugar, ya cake, ya honey, ya aishi koi cheez, jise “Marse Percy mind ya miss nahi karenge,” lekin paise nahi—kabhi ek cent bhi nahi. Woh apne mukarno (protestations) mein kaafi kushal the, lekin Mr. Driscoll unse hile nahi. Unhone badle mein har ek ko ek karrwe (stern) “Chor ka naam batao!” ke sath javab diya.

Truth yeh tha, Roxana ke alava saare guilty the; unhein shak tha ki doosre guilty hain, lekin woh nishchitta se nahi jaanti thin ki aisa hai. Woh yeh soch kar horrified thin ki woh khud guilty hone ke kitne paas aa gayi thin; unhein do hafte pehle colored Methodist Church mein ek revival (dharmik jaagran) ke zariye sahi mauqe par (in the nick of time) bachaya gya tha, jis samay aur jagah unhein “religion mila” (got religion) tha. Us gracious experience ke theek agle din, jab unke style ka badlav unpar fresh tha aur unhein apni purified condition par ghamand (vain) tha, unke master ne unke desk par ek-do dollars unprotected chhode the, aur jab woh dust-rag ke sath chaaron taraf polish kar rahi thin toh woh us temptation (laalach) se takra gain. Unhone thodi der tak ek lagaatar badhte hue krodh (rising resentment) ke sath paise ko dekha, phir woh nikal padin—

"Dad blame dat revival, kaash ise kal tak ke liye put off (taal) diya gya hota!"

Phir unhone laalach dene wale (tempter) ko ek kitab se dhak diya, aur kitchen cabinet ke ek doosre member ko yeh mila. Unhone yeh balidan ek religious etiquette (dharmik shishtachar) ke mamle ke roop mein kiya; ek aishi cheez jo abhi ke liye zaroori thi, lekin kisi bhi tarah se ise ek precedent (purv-nazeer) mein nahi badla jana tha; nahi, ek-do hafte unqi dharmikta ko lachila (limber up) bana denge, phir woh dobara rational (tarkshastri) ho jayengi, aur agle do dollars jo thand mein baahir chhode jayenge unhein ek santusht karne wala (comforter) mil jayega—aur woh us comforter ka naam bata saktin thin.

Kya woh bad (kharab) thin? Kya woh apni race ke samanya hisse se badtar thin? Nahi. Unhein life ki battle mein ek unfair show mila tha, aur unka man'na tha ki dushman ka chote paimane par military advantage lena koi sin (paap) nahi hai; chote paimane par, bade par nahi. Jab bhi unhein chance milta, woh pantry se provisions churati (smouch) thin; ya ek brass thimble, ya ek cake of wax, ya ek emery-bag, ya needles ka ek paper, ya ek silver spoon, ya ek dollar bill, ya kapdo ke chote articles, ya halki keemat ki koi doosri property; aur is tarah un reprisal (badle ki karvaai) ko paap-purna maanne se door thin, ki woh church jaati thin aur apni pockets mein loot ke saaman (plunder) ke sath sabse tez aur sabse sincere chillati aur pray karti thin. Ek farm ke smoke-house ko bhaari padlock lagakar rakhna padta tha, kyunki colored deacon khud bhi ek ham (maans) ka virodh nahi kar sakte the jab Providence ne unhein ek dream mein, ya otherwise, dikhaya ki aishi cheez kahan lonesome latki hai aur kisi ke pyaar ke liye taras rahi hai. Lekin apne samne ek sau latke hone par deacon do nahi lete the—yaani, same raat ko. Barfeele raaton (frosty nights) mein dayalu negro prowler (chori-chupke ghoomne wala mard) ek takhte ke end ko garm karta aur ise tree mein roosting (baithe) chickens ke cold claws ke neeche rakh deta; ek drowsy (neend mein) hen us comfortable board par step rakhti, softly kukur-ku karke apni kritagyata (gratitude) dikhati, aur prowler use apne bag mein dump kar deta, aur baad mein apne stomach mein, poori tarah se sure hote hue ki us insaan se is mamuli cheez ko lene mein jo daily usse ek amoolya khazane—unki aazaadi (liberty)—ko loot-ta hai, woh aisa koi sin nahi kar raha tha jise God Last Great Day (aakhiri faisale ke din) unke khilaf yaad rakkhega.

"Chor ka naam batao!"

Chauthi baar Mr. Driscoll ne aisa kaha tha, aur hamesha usi same hard tone mein. Aur ab unhone bhaari mahatva (awful import) ke yeh sabd add kiye:

"Main aapko ek minute deta hoon"—unhone apna watch baahar nikaala. "Agar us samay ke ant tak aapne confess (swikar) nahi kiya, toh main na keval aap charon ko bech dunga, balki—**main unhein RIVER KE NEECHE (DOWN THE RIVER) bech dunga!**"

Yeh unhein hell (narak) bhejne ke barabar tha! Kisi Missouri negro ko ispar shakk nahi tha. Roxy apni jagah par ladkhadayi aur unke face se color vanished (ud) gya; doosre ghutno ke bal aise gir pade jaise unhein shot kiya gya ho; unki aankhon se aansu nikal pade, unke supplicating hands (prarthna karte haath) upar uthe, aur ek hi instant mein teen answers aaye:

"Maine kiya hai!"

"Maine kiya hai!"

"Maine kiya hai!—reham karein, master—Lord reham karein hum poor niggers par!"

"Very good," master ne apna watch wapas rakhte hue kaha, "main tumhein yahin bech dunga bhale hi tum iske layak nahi ho. Tumhein river ke neeche hi becha jana chahiye."

Doshiyon (culprits) ne kritagyata ke ek utsah (ecstasy of gratitude) mein khud ko prone (dandvat) phenk diya, aur unke pairon ko kiss kiya, declare karte hue ki woh unqi goodness ko kabhi nahi bhoolenge aur jab tak zinda rahenge unke liye pray karna kabhi band nahi karenge. Woh sincere the, kyunki ek bhagwan ki tarah unhone apna mighty haath badhaya tha aur unke khilaf hell ke gates ko close kar diya tha. Woh khud jaante the ki unhone ek umda aur gracious cheez ki hai, aur apni is udaarta (magnanimity) se personally achhi tarah khush the; aur us raat unhone is incident ko apni diary mein likha, taaki unka son aane wale saalon mein ise padh sake, aur isse khud gentleness aur humanity ke deeds karne ke liye prerit (moved) ho sake.

---

## The 9 Principles Checklist of Ultralearning

*(In-Context Strategy Alignment Review)*

David Wilson ke fingerprint records lene aur James Clear ke Atomic Habits ke spaced learning ko is chapter ki ghatnaon se jodte hue, learning efficiency ko barkarar rakhne ke liye apni checklist ko monitor karein:

* **[ ] 1. Metalearning (First Draw a Map):** Wilson ne bacchon ke finger-marks ki ek niyamit "series" plan ki, jo long-term tracking ke liye data mapping ka sahi use pradarshit karti hai.
* **[ ] 2. Focus (Sharpen Your Knife):** Jasper kaam shuru karne se pehle dhoop mein aaram kar raha tha—procrastination ke is conscious loop ko recognize karke 10-minute struggle timer se overcome karein.
* **[ ] 3. Directness (Go Straight Ahead):** Roxy ne kanooni aur samajik boundaries ke direct context ko samajh kar apne bolne ke tareeqe ko badla, jo real-world constraints ke mutabik dhalne ka example hai.
* **[ ] 4. Drill (Attack Your Weakest Point):** Driscoll ne chor ko pakadne ke liye pure household ko summon kiya; jab complex patterns mein bottleneck ho, toh subcomponents par kade kadam uthaein.
* **[ ] 5. Retrieval (Test to Learn):** Wilson ne glass strips par marks lene ke baad unhein manually paper par copy aur pantograph se enlarge kiya taaki memory ke abstract visual patterns ko bina hints ke accurately process kar sakein.

---

# Chapter III — Roxy Plays a Shrewd Trick

### *(Roxy Ek Chalaki-Bhari Chaal Chalti Hai)*

---

> *Whoever has lived long enough to find out what life is, knows how deep a debt of gratitude we owe to Adam, the first great benefactor of our race. He brought death into the world.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Jis kisi ne bhi life kya hai yeh jaan'ne jitna lamba jee liya hai, woh jaanta hai ki hum Adam ke kitne gehre aabhari hain, jo hamari race ke pehle sabse bade upkaari [benefactor] the. Woh duniya mein maut lekar aaye.)*

---

Percy Driscoll us raat achhi tarah soye jis raat unhone apne ghar ke gulamon (house-minions) ka river ke neeche beche jaane se bachaav kiya, lekin Roxy ki aankhon mein neend ki ek jhapki tak nahi aayi. Ek gehre darr (profound terror) ne unpar kabza kar liya tha. Unka bachha bada hokar river ke neeche becha ja sakta tha! Is vichaar ne unhein darr se paagal (crazed) kar diya tha. Agar woh thoda soti thin aur ek moment ke liye khoto (lost herself) jaatin, toh agle hi moment woh apne pairon par khadi hokar apne bache ke palne (cradle) ki taraf bhaagti thin yeh dekhne ke liye ki kya yeh abhi bhi wahan hai ya nahi. Phir woh use apne dil se laga letin (gather it to her heart) aur chummon ke ek pagalpan (frenzy of kisses) mein uspar apna pyaar undel detin, karahti, roti, aur kehti, "Woh nahi karenge, oh, woh nahi karenge!—tumhari poor mammy tumhein pehle hi maar degi!"

Ek baar, jab woh use wapas uske palne mein tuck (laga) rahi thin, toh doosre bache ne apni neend mein thoda halchal (nestled) kiya aur unka dhayan apni taraf kheencha. Woh gayi aur ek lambe samay tak uske upar khadi hokar apne aap se baatcheet (communing) karne lagi:

"Mere poor baby ne kya kiya hai, jo use tumhari jaisi kismat (luck) nahi mil sakti thi? Usne kuch nahi kiya hai. God tumhare prati achhe the; woh uske prati achhe kyun nahi the? Woh tumhein river ke neeche nahi bech sakte. Mujhe tumhare pappy se nafrat hai; unke paas koi dil nahi hai—kam se kam niggers ke liye toh bilkul nahi. Mujhe unse nafrat hai, aur main unhein maar sakti hoon!" Woh thodi der ruki, sochti hui; phir woh dobara behad rone (wild sobbings) mein nikal padin, aur door mud gayi, kehti hui, "Oh, mujhe apne bache ko maarna hoga, koi doosra raasta nahi hai,—use maarna bache ko river ke neeche jaane se nahi bachayega. Oh, mujhe yeh karna hoga, tumhari poor mammy ko tumhein bachane ke liye tumhein maarna hoga, honey"—unhone ab apne baby ko apni chaati se laga liya (gathered her baby to her bosom), aur dulaaron ke sath use smother (sokhne/gale lagane) lagi—"Mammy ko tumhein maarna hoga—main ise kaise kar sakti hoon! Lekin tumhari mammy tumhein chhodne wali (desert) nahi hai—nahi, nahi; dah, ro mat—woh aapke sath ja rahi hai, woh khud ko bhi maar degi. Chalo, honey, mammy ke sath chalo; hum river mein jump karne ja rahe hain, phir is duniya ki saari troubles khatam ho jayengi—woh poor niggers ko wahan door river ke neeche nahi bechte."

Woh door ki taraf badhi, bache ke liye gungunati hui (crooning) aur use chup karwati hui; beech raaste mein woh sudden ruk gayi. Unqi nazar apni nayi Sunday gown par padi thi—ek sasti curtain-calico (parde ke kapde) ki cheez, bhadkeele rangon aur kaalpnik aakritiyon (fantastic figures) ka ek jhonka (conflagration). Unhone iska utsah se (wistfully/opulently) moolyankan kiya:

"Ise abhi tak kabhi nahi pehna hai," unhone kaha, "aur yeh bahut lovely hai." Phir unhone ek pleasant idea ke response mein apna head hilaaya, aur add kiya, "Nahi, main is misable purane linsey-woolsey (saste unee kapde) mein baahar nahi nikaali (fished out) jaungi, jabki har koi mujhe dekh raha ho."

Unhone bache ko neeche rakkha aur kapde badal liye. Unhone glass mein dekha aur apni beauty par hairan (astonished) thin. Unhone apni maut ke sringaar (death-toilet) ko perfect banane ka nishchay kiya. Unhone apne handkerchief-turban ko utara aur apne chamkile vishal baalon (glossy wealth of hair) ko "safed logon" (white folks) ki tarah banaya; unhone thode alag-alag bhaag (odds and ends) ke roop mein kaafi bhadkeele ribbon (lurid ribbon) aur ek kharab lagne wale artificial flowers ke guchhe ko add kiya; finally unhone apne kandhoon par ek fluffy cheez phenki jise un dino "cloud" (ek tarah ka shawl) kaha jata tha, jo ek blazing red rang ka tha. Phir woh qabr (tomb) ke liye ready thin.

Unhone ek baar phir apne baby ko ikhatha kiya; lekin jab unqi nazar uske behad chote chote gray tow-linen shirt par padi aur unhone uski gareeb jhajharata (pauper shabbiness) aur apne khud ke narki shandariyon ke is jwalamukhi ubaal (volcanic irruption of infernal splendors) ke beech ke farq (contrast) ko notice kiya, toh unka maa ka dil pighal (touched) gya, aur unhein sharm aayi.

"Nahi, dolling, mammy tumhare sath aisa bhed-bhav nahi karne wali hai. Angels tumhein utna hi admire (sarahenge) karenge jitna woh tumhari mammy ko karte hain. Aisa nahi hone wala hai ki woh apni aankhon ke samne apne haath rakhien aur David aur Goliah aur un doosre prophets se kahein, 'Uss bache ne is jagah ke hisab se bahut zyaada asabhya kapde (dressed too indelicate) pehne hain.'"

Is samay tak unhone shirt ko utar diya tha. Ab unhone us bare (nange) chote prani ko Thomas à Becket ke snowy long baby-gowns mein se ek pehna diya, jisme bright blue bows aur ruffles ki dainty flummery (naazuk dikhava) thi.

"Dah—now you’s fixed (ab tum taiyar ho)." Unhone bache ko ek chair par tikaya (propped) aur iska moolyankan karne ke liye door khadi ho gayin. Turant unqi aankhein hairani (astonishment) aur admiration se widen hone lagin, aur unhone apne haath thapathapaye (clapped her hands) aur chilla uthin, "Why, yeh toh sabse behtar (beat all) hai!—main kabhi nahi jaanti thi ki tum itne lovely ho. Marse Tommy ek bit bhi puttier (sundar) nahi hai—ek single bit bhi nahi."

Woh ek kadam aage badhin aur doosre infant (shishu) par ek nazar daali; unhone apne khud ke bache par ek glance peeche phenki; phir ek aur nazar ghar ke waaris (heir of the house) par daali. Ab unqi aankhon mein ek naya rahasyamai raasta sanket (strange light dawned) hua, aur ek moment mein woh vicharon mein doob gayin. Woh ek trance (moorchha) mein lagti thin; jab woh isse baahar aayin toh woh bhurbhurayin, "Jab main kal unhein tub mein dho (awashin') rahi thin, toh uske apne pappy ne mujhse poocha tha ki unmein se kaun sa unka hai."

Woh ek dream mein majood insaan ki tarah chaaron taraf move karne lagin. Unhone Thomas à Becket ke kapde utare, use har ek cheez se nanga (stripping) kar diya, aur uspar tow-linen shirt pehna di. Unhone uske coral necklace ko apne khud ke bache ke neck par pehna diya. Phir unhone bacchon ko side by side (sath-sath) rakkha, aur gombhir moolyankan (earnest inspection) ke baad woh bhurbhurayin—

"Ab kaun vishwas karega ki kapde (clo'es) aisa kuch kar sakte hain? Dog my cats agar main khud ek ko doosre se alag pehchanne (tell t'other fum which) ke liye struggle na karoon, uske pappy ki toh baat hi chodo."

Unhone apne bache (cub) ko Tommy ke elegant palne mein rakkha aur kaha—

"Tum ab se young Marse Tom ho, aur mujhe iska abhyas (practise) karna hoga aur tumhein us naam se pukaarna yaad rakhne ke liye used to (aadi) banna hoga, honey, ya main kabhi koi galti kar baithungi aur hum dono ko trouble mein daal dungi. Dah—now you lay still (ab shaant leto) aur mazeed chid-chide (fret) mat ho, Marse Tom—oh, heaven mein good Lord ko thank you, tum bach gaye, tum bach gaye!—ab aisa koi mard nahi hai jo mammy ke poor chote honey ko river ke neeche bech sake!"

Unhone ghar ke waaris (heir of the house) ko apne bache ke bina paint kiye pine ke palne mein rakkha, aur uski soti hui aakriti (slumbering form) ko uneasily dekhte hue kaha—

"Mujhe tumhare liye dukh hai, honey; mujhe dukh hai, God jaanta hai main hoon,—lekin main kya kar sakti hoon, main kya kar sakti thi? Tumhare pappy use kisi na kisi ko bech dete, kisi samay, aur phir woh nishchit roop se (sho') river ke neeche chala jata, aur main ise bardaasht nahi kar sakti thi, nahi kar sakti thi, nahi kar sakti thi."

Unhone apne aap ko apne bed par phenk diya aur sochne aur karvatein badalane (toss and think, think and toss) lagin. Thodi der mein woh sudden seedhe baith gayin (sat upright), kyunki ek santusht karne wala vichaar (comforting thought) unke chintit mind ke beech se nikaala tha—

"Yeh koi sin (paap) nahi hai—safed logon (white folks) ne ise kiya hai! Yeh koi paap nahi hai, glory to goodness yeh koi paap nahi hai! Unhone ise kiya hai—haan, aur woh poore dher mein sabse bade quality (highest class) wale the—kings!"

Woh vicharon mein doobne lagin; woh apni memory se us kahani ke dhundhle details (dim particulars) ikhatha karne ki koshish kar rahi thin jise unhone kabhi na kabhi suna tha. Aakhirkar unhone kaha—

"Ab mujhe yeh mil gaya hai; ab mujhe yaad (remember) aaya. Yeh us purane nigger preacher ne bataya tha, jab woh Illinois se yahan aaye the aur nigger church mein bhashan (preached) diya tha. Unhone kaha tha ki koi bhi apne aap ko khud nahi bacha sakta—bina vishwas (faith) ke nahi kar sakta, bina kaamon (works) ke nahi kar sakta, kisi bhi tareeqe se bilkul nahi kar sakta. Free grace (muft kripa) hi akela raasta hai, aur woh kisi se nahi milti siwaye Lord ke; aur woh ise jise chahein de sakte hain, saint ho ya sinner—unhein parwah nahi hai. Woh wahi karte hain jaisa unka dimaag (mineter) ho. Woh kisi ko bhi select (s'lect out) kar lete hain jo unhein suit kare, aur uski jagah par ek doosre ko rakh dete hain, aur pehle wale ko hamesha ke liye happy kar dete hain aur doosre ko Satan ke sath jalne ke liye chhod dete hain. Preacher ne kaha tha ki yeh exactly waisa hi hai jaisa unhone Englan' mein ek baar kiya tha, bahut samay pehle. Queen ne ek din apne baby ko aise hi rakkha chhod diya, aur baahar chali gayin; aur us jagah ke aas-paas ke niggers mein se ek jo lagbhag white thi, woh andar aayi aur usne dekha ki bacha aise hi leta hai, aur usne apne bache ke kapde queen ke bache par pehna diye, aur queen ke bache ke kapde apne bache par pehna diye, aur phir apne bache ko wahan leta chhod diya aur queen ke bache ko nigger-quarter (gulamon ke ilaqe) mein apne ghar le aayi, aur kisi ko kabhi pata nahi chala, aur uska bacha jaldi hi king ban gaya, aur usne ek baar queen ke bache ko river ke neeche bech diya jab unhein property ka hisab (settle up de estate) karna tha. Dah, now—preacher ne khud aisa kaha tha, aur yeh koi paap nahi hai, kyunki white folks ne ise kiya hai. Unhone ise kiya hai—haan, unhone ise kiya hai; aur na keval khali common white folks ne balki poore dher mein jo sabse badi quality (highest class) hai unhone. Oh, main bahut glad hoon ki mujhe us baare mein yaad aaya!"

Woh light-hearted (halke dil) aur happy hokar uthin, aur palno ke paas gayin aur raat ka bacha hua hissa **"abhyas (practising)"** karne mein spend kiya. Woh apne bache ko ek halka pat (thapthapahat) detin aur vinamra roop se kehtin, "Shant leto, Marse Tom," phir asli Tom ko ek pat detin aur karrwai (severity) se kehtin, "Shant leto, Chambers!—kya tum chahte hoon ki main tumhare sath kuch karoon?"

Jaise-jaise woh apni practice ke sath progress karti gayin, woh yeh dekhkar hairan thin ki jis darr-shradha (awe) ne unqi tongue ko reverent (sammanit) aur unke tareeqe ko apne young master ke prati humble rakkha tha, woh tezi se aur nishchitta se (steadily and surely) us kapat-veshi/gair-kanooni kabza karne wale (usurper) ke prati unke bolne aur tareeqe mein transfer ho raha tha, aur kaise similarly handy woh Driscoll ke purane ghar ke badkismat waaris (unlucky heir) ke prati apne maa ke bolne ke karrwe-pan (curtness) aur tareeqe ke aadesh-shahi (peremptoriness) ko transfer karne mein ban rahi thin.

Woh practice se kabhi-kabhi aaram (rests) letin, aur apne chances ko calculate karne mein absorbed (leeng) ho jaatin.

"Woh aaj in niggers ko paise churane ke liye bech denge, phir woh kuch aur buy karenge jo bacchon ko nahi jaante—toh woh sab right hai. Jab main bacchon ko hawa lagane (git de air) ke liye baahar le jaungi, toh jaise hi main kone par hungi main unke mouths ke chaaron taraf jam lapet (gaum) dungi, phir koi notice nahi kar sakta ki unhein badla gya hai. Haan, main aisa karne wali hoon jab tak main safe na ho jaoon, bhale hi ek saal lage.

"Wahan sirf ek hi mard hai jisse main darti (afeard) hoon, aur woh hai woh Pudd’nhead Wilson. Woh use pudd’nhead kehte hain, aur kehte hain ki woh bewakoof hai. My lan', woh mard isse zyaada bewakoof nahi hai jitni main hoon! Woh is town ka sabse smartest mard hai, jab tak ki yeh Jedge Driscoll ya maybe Pem Howard na hon. Blame dat man, woh mujhe apne un bekar chashmon (ornery glasses) se pareshan karta hai; mera vishwas hai ki woh ek witch (jaadugar) hai. Lekin nemmine (parwah nahi), main in dino mein se kisi din wahan jaungi aur aisa dikhava (let on) karungi ki main sochti hoon ki woh bacchon ke fingers ko phir se print karna chahte hain; aur agar unhone notice nahi kiya ki unhein badla gya hai, main bound hoon ki koi bhi ise notice nahi karne wala hai, aur phir main safe hoon, sho'. Lekin main sochti hoon ki main witch-work (jaadu-tona) ko door rakhne ke liye ek hoss-shoe (ghode ki naal) sath le jaungi."

Naye negroes ne Roxy ko beshak koi trouble nahi di. Master ne unhein koi trouble nahi di, kyunki unke speculations (vyapar) mein se ek khatre (jeopardy) mein tha, aur unka mind itna occupied tha ki unhone bacchon ko mushkil se dekha jab unhone unqi taraf glance kiya, aur Roxy ko bas itna karna tha ki jab woh aas-paas aayein toh un dono ko hansi ke ek jhonke (gale of laughter) mein la de; phir unke faces mukhya roop se masoodon (gums) ko expose karne wali cavities (khaali jagah) hote the, aur woh isse pehle ki spasm (hansi ka daura) guzar jaye aur chote prani ek insani roop (human aspect) dobara le lein, wapas chale jaate the.

Kuch hi dino mein us speculation ki kismat itni sandehjanak (dubious) ho gayi ki Mr. Percy apne bhai Judge ke sath chale gaye, yeh dekhne liye ki is baare mein kya kiya ja sakta hai. Yeh hamesha ki tarah ek jameen ka vyapar (land speculation) tha, aur yeh ek lawsuit (kanooni mukadme) ke sath complicated ho gya tha. Mard saat hafte (seven weeks) tak baahar rahe. Unke wapas lautne se pehle Roxy ne Wilson ke yahan apni visit kar li thi, aur satisfied thin. Wilson ne finger-prints liye, unpar names aur date—October the first—ke sath label lagaya, unhein saavdhani se door rakkha aur Roxy ke sath apni chat jaatri rakhi, jo is baare mein bahut zyaada anxious lag rahi thin ki woh bacchon ke flesh aur beauty mein hui badi progress ko admire karein jo bacchon ne ek mahine pehle unke finger-prints lene ke baad se ki thi. Unhone unqi improvement ki tareef ki jisse unhein santoosh (contentment) mila; aur chunki woh jam ya kisi doosre daag ke kisi bhi disguises ke bina the, woh poore samay tremble (kaanp) rahi thin aur miserably frightened (pareshan roop se dari hui) thin ki kahin kisi bhi moment woh—

Lekin unhone aisa nahi kiya. Unhone kuch bhi discover nahi kiya; aur woh jubilant (ullasit) hokar ghar gayin, aur us mamle ke baare mein saari chinta ko permanently apne mind se chhod diya.

---

## The 9 Principles Checklist of Ultralearning

*(In-Context Strategy Alignment Review)*

Roxy ke is chalaki-bhare trick (shrewd trick) aur dimaagi badlavon ko dekh kar, learning retention aur behavior refinement ke mutabik apni strategy checklist ko review karein:

* **[ ] 1. Metalearning (First Draw a Map):** Roxy ne dhoondh-dhoondh kar purani tales aur preaching ke map ko memory se nikala, jo jankari ke different layers (metadata) ko filter karne ka achha pradarshan hai.
* **[ ] 2. Focus (Sharpen Your Knife):** Roxy ne poori raat bina soye bacchon ke behavior badlav par focus kiya; bhatkaav ke sroton (jaise apni nayi gown ka lalach) ko temporarily side rakh kar mukhya objective par tike rahin.
* **[ ] 3. Directness (Go Straight Ahead):** Swa-shiksha ke ziye Roxy ne "safed logon" ke bolne aur nirdesh dene ke tareeqe (peremptoriness of manner) ki direct practice shuru ki taaki identity badlav real-world context mein seamless lage.
* **[ ] 4. Drill (Attack Your Weakest Point):** "Marse Tom" aur "Chambers" pukaarne ke apne kamzor points ko identify karke, unhone raat bhar unhi vishisht subskills ko baar-baar drill kiya taaki future mein galti na ho.
* **[ ] 5. Retrieval (Test to Learn):** Wilson ke yahan wapas jaakar bacchon ke naye finger-prints dena aur yeh test karna ki kya woh badlav ko pakad paata hai ya nahi, closed-book condition mein apni safety ko check karne ka sateek tareeqa tha.

---

# Chapter IV — The Ways of the Changelings

### *(Badle Gaye Bacchon Ke Tareeqe)*

---

> *Adam and Eve had many advantages, but the principal one was, that they escaped teething.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Adam aur Eve ke paas kai fayde the, lekin mukhya fayda yeh tha ki woh daant nikalne [teething] ki takleef se bach gaye.)*
> *There is this trouble about special providences—namely, there is so often a doubt as to which party was intended to be the beneficiary. In the case of the children, the bears and the prophet, the bears got more real satisfaction out of the episode than the prophet did, because they got the children.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Khas tarah ki kripa [special providences] ke sath yeh problem hai—yaani, aksar is baat par shakk hota hai ki kis paksh ko labh-arthi [beneficiary] banana taye tha. Bacchon, bears aur prophet ke mamle mein, bears ko us episode se prophet ke mukable mazeed asli satisfaction mila, kyunki unhein bache mil gaye the.)*

---

Is history ko ab se us badlav (change) ke mutabik khud ko dhalna (accommodate) hoga jise Roxana ne anjam diya (consummated) hai, aur asli waaris ko “Chambers” aur kapat-veshi chote gulam (usurping little slave) ko “Thomas à Becket” pukaarna hoga—rozmarra ke use ke liye is baad wale naam ko chhota karke “Tom” karte hue, jaisa unke aas-paas ke log karte the.

“Tom” apni kapat (usurpation) ke shuruat se hi ek kharab baby tha. Woh bina kisi baat ke rota; woh bina kisi notice ke shaitani gusse ke toofano (storms of devilish temper) mein phat padta, aur ek ke baad ek shriek (chillaahat) aur howl (rona) chhodta, phir daant nikalne wale shishu (teething nursling) ki us dravni vishesta (frightful specialty) ke sath us cheez ko climax par le jata jisme woh apna saans rok leta (holding his breath), jiske dard mein woh prani apne lungs ko thaka deta, phir apna saans wapas paane ke prayas mein bina awaaz ke machalne (squirmings), marodne (twistings) aur pair phenkne (kickings) ke sath kaanp uthta, jabki lips blue ho jaate aur mouth poori tarah se wide aur rigid (sakht) khada rehta, laal masoodon ke ek ghere ke neeche ke rim mein sthit ek chote se daant (wee tooth) ko jaanch ke liye prastut karte hue; aur jab woh daravni khamoshi (appalling stillness) tab tak barkarar rehti jab tak koi sure na ho jaye ki khoya hua saans kabhi wapas nahi lautega, tab ek nurse udti hui aati, aur bache ke face par paani ke chhete maarti, aur—presto (turant)! lungs bhar jaate, aur instantly ek shriek, ya ek yell, ya ek howl discharge karte jo sunne wale ke kaan phad deta aur uske malik ko aise sabd bolne par hairan (surprises) kar deta jo halo (bhavya-ghera) ke sath sui-suited nahi hote agar uske paas ek hota. Baby Tom kisi ko bhi noch (claw) leta jo uske nails ki reach mein aata, aur apni rattle (jhunjhuna) se kisi ko bhi peet (pound) deta jahan tak woh pahunch sakta. Woh paani ke liye tab tak chillata jab tak use yeh mil na jata, aur phir cup aur sab kuch floor par phenk deta aur mazeed ke liye chillata. Unki saari nakhre-baaziyon (caprices) ko jhela (indulged) jata, chahe woh kitni bhi pareshandar aur gussa dilane wali (troublesome and exasperating) kyun na hon; use jo kuch bhi woh chahta tha khane ki izazat thi, khhasakar aishi cheezein jo use stomach-ache (pet-dard) dengi.

Jab woh itna bada ho gya ki chaaron taraf ladkhada kar chalna (toddle about) shuru karein aur toote-phoote sabd bole aur ek idea haasil karein ki uske haath kis liye the, toh woh pehle se kahin zyaada ek poora kachra/pareshani (consummate pest) tha. Roxy ko koi aaram nahi milta tha jab tak woh jaag raha hota. Woh jo kuch bhi dekhta uske liye chillata, simply kehta “Awnt it!” (want it), jo ki ek command thi. Jab ise laya jata, toh woh ek pagalpan (frenzy) mein apne haathon se ise door karne ka sanket karte hue kehta, “Don’t awnt it! don’t awnt it!” aur jaise hi woh chala jata woh “Awnt it! awnt it! awnt it!” ki frantic yells shuru kar deta; aur Roxy ko apni heels ko pankh dene padte (give wings to her heels) the taaki us cheez ko uske paas wapas la sakein isse pehle ki use is baare mein convulsions (daure) mein jaane ke apne intention ko anjam dene ka samay mile.

Jo cheez woh saari doosri cheezon se upar prefer karta tha woh chimta (tongs) tha. Aisa isliye tha kyunki uske “father” ne use unhein lene se mana (forbidden) kiya tha taaki woh unse windows aur furniture na tode. Jaise hi Roxy ki peeth ghoomi woh chimte ke samne ladkhada kar jata aur kehta “Like it!” aur apni eye ko ek taraf karke dekhta ki kya Roxy notice kar rahi hai; phir, “Awnt it!” aur apni eye ko phir karke dekhta; phir, “Hab it!” ek aur chhupi hui nazar (furtive glance) ke sath; aur finally, “Take it!”—aur prize uska tha. Agle hi moment woh bhaari auzaar (heavy implement) upar uthaya jata; agle, ek dhamaka aur ek howl hota, aur cat ek mulaqat poori karne ke liye teen pairon par bhaag khadi hoti; Roxy theek tab pahuncheti jab lamp ya koi window na-sudharne yogya toot-phoot (irremediable smash) mein badal chuki hoti.

Tom ko saara dulaar (petting) milta tha, Chambers ko bilkul nahi. Tom ko saari delicacies (pakwan) miltin, Chambers ko mush (daliya) aur milk, aur bina sugar ke dahi (clabber). Nateejatan Tom ek bimar bacha (sickly child) tha aur Chambers nahi tha. Tom “fractious” (chid-chida) tha, jaisa Roxy ise kehti thin, aur dabdaba rakhne wala (overbearing); Chambers namra aur vineet (meek and docile) tha.

Apni saari shandaar samajh (splendid common sense) aur practical everyday ability ke bavajood, Roxy ek maa ke roop mein ek andhi pagal (doting fool of a mother) thin. Woh apne bache ke prati yeh thin—aur woh isse mazeed bhi thin: apne dwara create kiye gaye bhram (fiction) se, woh unka master ban gaya tha; is rishte ko baahri roop se recognize karne aur is recognition ko express karne ke liye required forms mein khud ko perfect banane ki zarurat ne unhein in forms ki practice karne mein aishi lagan aur vafadari (diligence and faithfulness) par dhakela ki is exercise ne jald hi khud ko aadat (habit) mein badal (concreted) liya; yeh automatic aur unconscious ho gya; phir ek natural result follow hua: kevel doosron ke liye intended dhoke (deceptions) gradually vyavaharik roop se khud ke dhoke (self-deceptions) bhi ban gaye; nakli darr-shradha (mock reverence) asli darr-shradha ban gayi, nakli chaploosi (mock obsequiousness) asli chaploosi ban gayi, nakli samman (mock homage) asli samman ban gaya; nakli gulam (imitation-slave) aur nakli master (imitation-master) ke beech ke batware ki woh choti nakli darar (counterfeit rift) wide aur wide hoti gayi, aur ek khaai (abyss) ban gayi, aur ek behad asli khaai—aur uske ek side par Roxy khadi thin, apne hi dhokon ki shikar (dupe), aur doosri taraf unka bacha khada tha, jo unke liye ab koi kapat-veshi (usurper) nahi tha, balki unka sweekar kiya gya aur recognized master tha. Woh unka darling, unka master, aur unki deity (devta) sab ek mein hi tha, aur uski apni pooja (worship) mein woh bhool gayin ki woh kaun thin aur woh kya raha tha.

Childhood mein Tom ne bina kisi daant (unrebuked) ke Chambers ko thappad maare, peeta aur nocha, aur Chambers ne jaldi hi seekh liya ki namrata se ise bardaasht karne (meekly bearing it) aur ispar krodh jatane (resenting it) ke beech, saara advantage pehle wali policy ke sath hi tha. Un kuch saalon mein jab unke utpeedan (persecutions) ne unhein control se baahar push kiya tha aur unhein fight back karne par majboor kiya tha, toh iski keemat unhein headquarters (mukhya karyalay/bhai ke yahan) par bahut bhaari chukani padi thi; Roxy ke haathon nahi, kyunki agar woh kabhi use is baat ke liye karrwai se daantne se aage jaanti thin ki woh “bhool gya (forgitt’n’) ki uska young master kaun tha,” toh woh kam se kam ek kaan par thappad (box on the ear) se aage apni punishment nahi badhati thin. Nahi, Percy Driscoll woh insaan the. Unhone Chambers ko bataya ki chahe koi bhi uksava (provocation) kyun na ho, use apne chote master ke khilaf haath uthane ka adhikaar nahi tha. Chambers ne teen baar line ko overstepped (paar) kiya, aur us mard se jinhone unke father hone ke bavajood yeh nahi jaanta tha, teen aishi convincing canings (bhaari pitaayi) haasil kin, ki usne uske baad poori namrata (all humility) mein Tom ke karrwe-pan ko jhela, aur koi naye experiments nahi kiye.

Ghar ke baahar dono boys apni poori boyhood ke dauran ek sath the. Chambers apni umra se pare strong tha, aur ek achha fighter tha; strong isliye kyunki use kachha khana (coarsely fed) diya jata tha aur ghar ke chaaron taraf hard kaam karwaya jata tha, aur ek achha fighter isliye kyunki Tom ne use abhyas ka ek vishal bhandar (plenty of practice) provide kiya tha—un white boys par jinse woh nafrat karta tha aur jinse darta tha. Chambers school aane-jaane ke dauran unka constant body-guard tha; woh recess mein playground par apne charge ko protect karne ke liye present rehta tha. Woh dhere-dhere fight karke ek aishi formidable reputation (daravni reputation) mein badal gya, ki Tom uske sath kapde badal sakta tha, aur “shanti se ride kar sakta tha,” jaise Sir Kay Laancelot ke armor (kawach) mein karte the.

Woh hunar ke games (games of skill) mein bhi achha tha. Tom use marbles (kanche) ke sath “keeps” (jeetne wala khel) khelne ke liye daanv par lagata (staked), aur phir saari winnings usse chheen leta. Sardi ke season mein Chambers taiyar rehta tha, Tom ke fate-purane kapdo mein, “holey” (chhed wale) red mittens, aur chhed wale shoes, aur knees aur seat par chhed wali pants pehan kar, Tom ke liye pahadi par ek sled khinchne ke liye, jo warm kapde pehne riding karne ke liye baithta; lekin use khud kabhi ride nahi mili. Unhone Tom ke nirdeshon (directions) ke tehat snow men aur snow fortifications (baraf ke kile) banaye. Woh Tom ka patient target (shant nishana) tha jab Tom baraf ke gole phenkna (snowballing) chahta tha, lekin target counter fire nahi kar sakta था. Chambers Tom ke skates ko river tak carry karta aur unhein uspar baandhta (strapped), phir ice par uske peeche-peeche ddauda, taaki zarurat padne par taiyar (on hand) reh sake; lekin use khud kabhi skates try karne ke liye nahi kaha gya.

Summer mein Dawson’s Landing ke boys ka pasandida bhatkaav (pet pastime) farmers ki fruit-wagons se apples, peaches, aur melons churana tha,—mukhya roop se us risk ke kaaran jo woh uthaate the ki farmer ke koode ke hassa (butt of the farmer's whip) se unka head khul sakta tha. Tom in thefts mein ek distinguished kushal (adept) mard tha—proxy (doosre ke zariye) ke zariye. Chambers unqi chori karta tha, aur apne hisse ke roop mein peach-stones, apple-cores, aur melon-rinds haasil karta tha.

Tom hamesha Chambers ko apne sath swimming mein le jata, aur ek protection ke roop mein apne paas rakhta. Jab Tom kaafi kar chuka hota, toh woh baahar nikal jata aur Chambers ki shirt mein knots (ganthe) baandh deta, knots ko paani mein dubo deta aur unhein kholne mein hard (hard to undo) bana deta, phir khud kapde pehan kar baith jata aur hansta jabki nanga kaanpne wala (naked shiverer) apne teeth se un ziddi knots (stubborn knots) ko khinchta.

Tom ne apne is mamuli saathi (humble comrade) ke sath yeh tarah-tarah ke ill turns (buraigaan) aashik roop se apni janmjaat shaitaniyat (native viciousness) se kiye, aur aashik roop se isliye kyunki woh uski physique aur sahas (pluck) ki superiorities, aur uski bahumukhi chaturai (manifold cleverness) ke kaaran usse nafrat karta tha. Tom dive nahi kar sakta tha, kyunki isse unhein sar-fatne-wala pet-pain (splitting headaches) hota tha. Chambers bina kisi asuvidha ke dive kar sakta tha, aur aisa karne ka shaukeen tha. Unhone ek din, white boys ki ek bheed ke beech, ek canoe (naav) ke stern se back somersaults (ulti palat) phenk kar itna mazeed admiration jagaya (excited), ki isne Tom ki aatma ko thaka diya (wearied Tom’s spirit), aur aakhirkar unhone canoe ko Chambers ke neeche dhakel diya jab woh hawa mein tha—isliye woh canoe-bottom mein apne head ke bal neeche aaya; aur jab woh unconscious leta tha, toh Tom ke kai purane virodhiyon (ancient adversaries) ne dekha ki unki lambi-chaahi umeed ka opportunity (long-desired opportunity) aa gya hai, aur unhone gair-kanooni waaris (false heir) ki aishi pitaayi (drubbing) ki ki Chambers ki sabse behtar madad ke sath bhi woh baad mein mushkil se khud ko ghar tak khinch paaye.

Jab boys fifteen aur usse upar ke the, Tom ek din river mein “show off” (dikhava) kar rahe the, tabhi unhein ek cramp (aithen) aayi, aur unhone madad ke liye shouted kiya. Yeh boys ke sath ek common trick thi—khhasakar agar koi stranger present ho—ek cramp ka pretend karna aur madad ke liye chillaana; phir jab stranger bachaav (rescue) ke liye tezi se badhta, toh chillaane wala tab tak struggle aur howl jaatri rakhta jab tak woh paas na ho jata, phir howl ko ek sarcastic smile se replace kar deta aur blandly door tair jata, jabki town ke boys shikar (dupe) par jeers (taano) aur hansi ki bauchhar kar dete. Tom ne is joke ko abhi tak try nahi kiya tha, sath hi mana gya ki woh abhi ise try kar rahe the, isliye boys saavdhani se peeche hat gaye; lekin Chambers ne vishwas kiya ki unke master sach mein (in earnest) hain, isliye woh tair kar baahar gaya, aur samay par pahuncha, unfortunately, aur unki life bacha li.

Yeh aakhiri tinka (last feather) tha. Tom ne baaki har ek cheez ko manage karke jhela tha, lekin publicly aur permanently ek nigger ke prati, aur saare niggers mein se is nigger ke prati aise ek aabhar (obligation) ke tehat rehna—yeh bahut zyaada tha. Unhone Chambers par madad ke liye pukaarne mein unke sach mein hone ke “pretending” (dikhava) karne ke liye insults ka dher laga diya, aur kaha ki ek block-headed nigger ke alava koi bhi jaan jata ki woh mazaak (funning) kar rahe the aur unhein akele chhod deta.

Tom ke enemies yahan strong force mein the, isliye woh apne opinions ke sath kaafi freely baahar aaye. Woh unpar hanste, aur unhein coward (darpok), liar (jhootha), sneak (chalu), aur doosre tarah ke pasandida naamon (pet names) se pukaarte, aur unhein bataya ki unka maqsad iske baad Chambers ko ek naye naam se pukaarna hai, aur ise town mein samanya banana hai—“Tom Driscoll’s niggerpappy (Tom Driscoll ka nigger-baap),” —yeh sanket dene ke liye ki unka is life mein ek doosra birth hua tha, aur Chambers unke naye being (vajood) ke author the.

Tom in taanton (taunts) ke tehat frantic (paagal) ho gaye, aur chilla uthe—

“Knock their heads off, Chambers! knock their heads off! Tum pockets mein haath daal kar wahan kyun khade ho?”

Chambers ne tark diya (expostulated), aur kaha, “Lekin, Marse Tom, unki sankhya bahut zyaada hai (dey’s too many)—woh—”

“Kya tum mujhe sun rahe ho?”

“Please, Marse Tom, mujhe majoor mat karein! Unki sankhya itni zyaada hai ki—”

Tom uspar jhapte (sprang at him) aur isse pehle ki boys unhein door khinch paate aur ghayal ladke (wounded lad) ko bach nikalne ka ek chance de paate, unhone apni pocket-knife do ya teen baar usme jhonk di. Use kaafi chot (considerably hurt) aayi thi, lekin seriously nahi. Agar blade thoda sa mazeed lamba hota toh unka career wahin khatam ho jata.

Tom ne bahut samay pehle Roxy ko “unki jagah (her place)” sikha di thi. Ab kai din ho gaye the jab unhone unke kshetra mein ek dulaar ya ek pasandida vishesan (fondling epithet) ki dharstata (ventured) ki thi. Ek “nigger” se aishi cheezein unke liye na-pasand (repulsive) thin, aur unhein apni distance maintain karne aur yaad rakhne ke liye warn kiya gya tha ki woh kaun thin. Unhone dekha ki unka darling gradually unka son banna band kar raha hai, unhone us detail ko poori tarah se nasht (perish utterly) hote dekha; jo kuch bacha tha woh master tha—master, pure aur simple, aur yeh koi naram mastership nahi thi, dono nahi. Unhone apne aap ko motherhood ki oonchi uunchei se gulamiyat ke gehre andhere (somber depths of unmodified slavery) mein doobte hue dekha. Unke aur unke boy ke beech ke batware ki khaai (abyss) complete thi. Woh ab merely unka saaman (chattel) thin, unqi suvidha, unka dog, unqi cringing aur helpless gulam, unke nakhre-baaz mizaj (capricious temper) aur shaitani nature ki ek vinamra aur virodh na karne wali victim.

Kabhi-kabhi fatigue (thakan) se thak jaane par bhi woh soo nahi saktin thin, kyunki unke boy ke sath din ke experiences par unka gussa bahut upar ubalta (rage boiled so high) tha. Woh apne aap se mumble aur mutter (bhurbhurati) karti thin—

"Usne mujhe maara, aur main kisi bhi tareeqe se doshi nahi thin—mujhe face par maara, theek logon ke samne. Aur woh mujhe hamesha nigger-wench, aur hussy, aur un saare mean naamon se pukaarta hai, jabki main apna sabse behtar (very bes') karne ki koshish kar rahi hoon. Oh, Lord, maine uske liye itna kuch kiya—maine use utha kar wahan tak pahunchaya jahan woh hai—aur yeh mujhe iske badle mila."

Kabhi-kabhi jab vishisht apmaan-janak (peculiar offensiveness) koi apmaan unke dil ko gehrai se kaat-ta, toh woh badle ke plans (schemes of vengeance) banatin aur duniya ke samne ek imposter (dhokebaaz) aur ek gulam ke roop mein uske expose hone ke kaalpnik pradarshan (fancied spectacle) mein doob jaatin; lekin in joys ke beech darr unhein hit karta: unhone use bahut zyaada strong bana diya tha; woh kuch bhi prove nahi kar saktin thin, aur—heavens, unhein unke prayason ke liye river ke neeche becha ja sakta tha! Toh unke plans hamesha bematlab jaate, aur woh unhein kismat ke khilaf, aur us ghaatank September din par ek gawah (witness) pradan na karne ke liye khud par ek bewakoof khelne (playing the fool) ke liye ek asamarth gusse (impotent rage) mein ek taraf rakh detin jiske upyog ki zarurat us din pad sakti hai jab unke badle ke bhookhe dil ko shaant (appeasing) karne ke liye aishi cheez ki zarurat ho.

Aur phir bhi jaise hi Tom unke prati kabhi achha, aur kind hota,—aur yeh har kuch samay baad hota tha,—unke saare dukh ke spots (sore places) heal ho jaate, aur woh happy ho jaatin; happy aur proud, kyunki yeh unka son تھا, unka nigger son, white logon ke beech dabdaba chalane wala aur unqi race ke khilaf unke crimes ka surakshit roop se badla lene wala.

Dawson’s Landing mein us sardi—1845 ki sardi—mein do bade janaze (grand funerals) hue. Ek Colonel Cecil Burleigh Essex ka tha, doosra Percy Driscoll ka.

Apni death-bed par Driscoll ne Roxy ko free kar diya aur apne idolized dikhne wale son (ostensible son) ko gombhirta se apne bhai, Judge aur unqi wife ke sahare (keeping) deliver kar diya. Un childless logon ko use paa kar khushi hui. Childless logon ko please karna difficult nahi hota.

Judge Driscoll ek mahine pehle, secretly apne bhai ke paas gaye the, aur Chambers ko kharid liya tha. Unhone suna tha ki Tom apne father ko bache ko river ke neeche bechne ke liye push karne ki koshish kar raha tha, aur woh is scandal ko rokna chahte the—kyunki public sentiment mamuli kaaran ya bina kisi kaaran ke family servants ke sath is tareeqe se treat karne ko approve nahi karta tha.

Percy Driscoll apne bade speculative jameen ke vyapar (speculative landed estate) ko bachane ki koshish mein khud ko thaka chuke the, aur bina successfully hue mar gaye the. Woh mushkil se apni qabr mein gaye the isse pehle ki boom collapsed (vyapar thapp) ho gya aur unke abhi tak ke envied (jalan-waale) young devil heir ko ek pauper (kangal) chhod diya. Lekin woh kuch nahi tha; unke uncle ne unhein bataya ki unhein unka heir banna chahiye aur marne par unqi saari fortune milni chahiye; toh Tom ko raahat (comforted) mili.

Roxy ke paas ab koi ghar nahi tha; isliye unhone apne doston ko good-by kehne ke liye chaaron taraf jaane aur phir baahar nikal kar duniya dekhne—yaani kehna ka matlab hai, ek steamboat par chambermaiding (naukrani ka kaam) karne ka nishchay kiya, jo unqi race aur ling ka darling ambition (sabse bada sapna) tha.

Unqi aakhiri call black giant, Jasper par thi. Unhone use Pudd’nhead Wilson ke sardi ke saaman ke liye lakdi kaat-te (chopping wood) hue paaya.

Wilson uske sath chat kar rahe the jab Roxy pahunchei. Unhone unse poocha ki woh chambermaiding par jaane aur apne boys ko chhodne ko kaise bardaasht kar sakti hain; aur mazaak mein (chaffingly) unke finger-prints ki ek series copy karne ka offer kiya, jo unke twelfth saal tak pahuncheti ho, unhein yaad rakhne ke liye; lekin woh ek moment mein shaant (sobered) ho gayin, hairan thin ki kya unhein kisi cheez par shak (suspected) hai; phir unhone kaha ki unka vishwas hai ki unhein unqi zarurat nahi hai. Wilson ne apne aap se kaha, “Usmein majood black blood ka qatra andh-vishwasi (superstitious) hai; woh sochti hai ki mere glass mystery ke baare mein kahin koi shaitaniyat, koi witch-business majood hai; woh yahan apne haath mein ek purane horseshoe ke sath aaya karti thin; yeh ek accident ho sakta tha, lekin mujhe isme shak hai.”

---

## The 9 Principles Checklist of Ultralearning

*(In-Context Strategy Alignment Review)*

Tom aur Chambers ke behavior badlavon aur Roxy ke dimaagi darr ko moolyankan karte hue, cognitive science ke principles ke mutabik apni strategy checklist ko review karein:

* **[ ] 1. Metalearning (First Draw a Map):** Tom ne apne choices ko systematically map kiya ki kab aur kaise bache ke roop mein chimte (tongs) par hamla karna hai jab Roxy ki peeth ghoomi ho.
* **[ ] 2. Focus (Sharpen Your Knife):** Chambers ne Tom ke orders ke tehat bina bhatke baraf ke kile (snow fortifications) banaye aur target ke roop mein bina counter fire kiye focus barkarar rakkha.
* **[ ] 3. Directness (Go Straight Ahead):** Tom ne thefts mein kushalata (adept) haasil karne ke liye proxy (Chambers) ka use kiya, jo directly results paane ke indirect shortcut ka udaharan hai.
* **[ ] 4. Drill (Attack Your Weakest Point):** Percy Driscoll se mili Convincing canings ne Chambers ke mind se virodh karne ke subcomponent ko completely mita diya, jisse usne Tom ke karrwe-pan ko hamesha ke liye jhela.
* **[ ] 5. Retrieval (Test to Learn):** Roxy ne kade environment mein galti se bachne ke liye raat bhar "Marse Tom" aur "Chambers" pukaarne ka abhyas kiya, jisse unke dimaag mein automatic response generate hua.
* **[ ] 6. Feedback (Don’t Dodge the Punches):** Tom ne public jeers aur taano (feedback) ke samna hone par gusse mein aakar Chambers par hamla kiya, ego ke beech mein aane se feedback ka galat use pradarshit hota hai.
* **[ ] 7. Retention (Don’t Fill a Leaky Bucket):** Wilson ne bacchon ke finger-prints ki 12th saal tak ki series ko space karke review karne ka offer kiya, jo long-term tracking ka sateek niyan hai.

---

# Chapter V — The Twins Thrill Dawson’s Landing

### *(Judwa Bhai Dawson’s Landing Ko Romanchit Karte Hain)*

---

> *Training is everything. The peach was once a bitter almond; cauliflower is nothing but cabbage with a college education.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Training hi sab kuch hai. Aadoo [peach] kabhi ek karrwa badaam tha; phool-gobi [cauliflower] aur kuch nahi balki college education paayi hui patta-gobi [cabbage] hai.)*
> *Remark of Dr. Baldwin’s, concerning upstarts: We don’t care to eat toadstools that think they are truffles.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Upstarts [nouveau riche/achanak ameer bane log] ke baare mein Dr. Baldwin ki tippani: Hum un kukurmutta [toadstools] ko khana pasand nahi karte jo khud ko truffles [ek qeemti jameen-kand] samajhte hain.)*

---

Mrs. York Driscoll ne us keemti inaam, Tom, ke sath do saal tak param anand (bliss) bhoga—yeh anand kabhi-kabar thoda chintit zoor hota tha, yeh sach hai, lekin phir bhi anand hi tha; phir woh mar gayin, aur unke husband aur unqi childless sister, Mrs. Pratt, ne usi purane stand (ghar) par anand ka yeh business jaatri rakkha. Tom ko unqi poori santushti tak—ya lagbhag us tak—bahut dulaara, laad kiya aur spoil (bighada) gya. Yeh tab tak chalta raha jab tak woh nineteen saal ke nahi ho gaye, aur phir unhein Yale bhej diya gya. Woh "sharton" (conditions) ke sath handsomely equipped hokar gaye, lekin otherwise woh wahan kisi vishishtata ya charcha (object of distinction) ke patra nahi the. Woh do saal tak Yale mein rahe, aur phir unhone us sangharsh ko chhod (threw up the struggle) diya. Woh apne tareeqon mein kaafi behtar badlav (improved manners) lekar ghar laute; unhone apna chid-chidapan aur rukha-pan (surliness and brusqueness) kho diya tha, aur ab woh kaafi pleasantly soft aur smooth the; woh chhupkar, aur kabhi-kabhi openly, vyang-bhari bhasha (ironical of speech) bolte the, aur logon ke dukhhte rag (touching people on the raw) ko halke se chhoone ke aadi the, lekin woh aisa ek good-natured aur semiconscious air (bina-parwah wale dhang) se karte the jo ise surakshit roop se carry off kar leta tha, aur unhein trouble mein padne se bachata tha. Woh pehle ki tarah hi aalsi (indolent) the aur unhone koi bahut tivra desire nahi dikhai kisi occupation (kaam-dhandhe) ko dhoondhne ki. Logon ne isse tark nikaala ki woh tab tak apne uncle ke sahare rehna prefer karte the jab tak ki unke uncle ke jootey khaali na ho jayein (yaani unki maut na ho jaye). Woh apne sath ek-do nayi habits lekar aaye the, jinmein se ek ka woh kaafi openly abhyas karte the—tippling (sharab-noshi)—lekin doosri ko chhupakar rakhte the jo gambling (jua) thi. Jahan unke uncle is baare mein sun sakein wahan jua khelna kaam nahi karega; woh yeh kaafi achhi tarah jaante the.

Tom ka yeh Eastern polish (shehri chamak) young logon ke beech popular nahi tha. Woh ise shayad bardaasht kar lete, agar Tom yahin ruk jata; lekin woh gloves (dastaane) pehnta tha, aur ise woh bardaasht nahi kar sakte the, aur nahi karenge; isliye woh mukhya roop se samaj (society) ke bina hi tha. Woh apne sath ek aisa kapdo ka suit ghar lekar aaya jiska style, cut aur fashion itna umda tha,—Eastern fashion, shehri fashion,—ki isne har kisi ko kasht (anguish) se bhar diya aur ise ek vishisht roop se dharstata-bhara apmaan (wanton affront) maana gya.
