Woh us feeling ka anand le raha tha jise woh jagah raha tha, aur poore din serene aur happy hokar town mein parade karta tha; lekin young bandon ne us raat ek tailor ko kaam par laga diya, aur jab Tom agle subah apni parade par nikla toh usne paaya ki ek purana, apang negro bell-ringer (ghaanti bajane wala gulam) uske piche-piche ladkhada kar chal (straddling along) raha hai, jo uske kapdo ki shandari ke ek bhadkeele parde-ke-kapde wale badha-chadhakar kiye gaye roop (flamboyant curtain-calico exaggeration) mein saja (tricked out) hua tha, aur jitna behtar woh kar sakta tha uske fancy Eastern graces ki nakal kar raha tha.

Tom ne surrender (haar maan) kar diya, aur uske baad khud ko local fashion ke mutabik kapde pehnaaye. Lekin woh dull country town unqi shehri kshetron (livelier regions) ke parichay ke baad se unke liye tiresome (ubau) tha, aur yeh daily mazeed se mazeed waisa hi hota gya. Unhone refreshment (manoranjan) ke liye St. Louis ke chote trips karna shuru kar diya. Wahan unhein apne mutabik saathi (companionship) mile, aur unqi taste ke pleasures, sath hi kuch mamlon mein mazeed freedom bhi mili, usse kahin zyaada jitni unhein ghar par mil sakti thi. So, agle do saalon ke dauran city mein unqi visits ki frequency badh gayi aur unka wahan rukna (tarryings) steadily samay ke mamle mein lamba hota gya.

Woh gehre paani (deep waters/mushkil) mein utar rahe the. Woh secretly aise chances le rahe the jo unhein kisi din trouble mein daal sakte the—in fact, daal diya.

Judge Driscoll 1850 mein bench se aur saari business activities ke sath retire ho chuke the, aur ab teen saal se comfortably aalsi (idle) the. Woh *Free-thinkers’ Society* ke president the, aur Pudd’nhead Wilson doosre member the. Society ke weekly discussions ab us purane lawyer ki life ke mukhya interest the. Pudd’nhead abhi bhi seedhi (ladder) ke bottom par andhere (obscurity) mein ghisaai kar rahe the, us badkismat tippani ke shraap (blight) ke tehat jise unhone twenty-three saal pehle dog ke baare mein chhod diya tha.

Judge Driscoll unke dost the, aur claim karte the ki unke paas average se upar ka mind hai, lekin ise Judge ke nakhron (whims) mein se ek maana gya, aur yeh public opinion ko badalane mein fail raha. Ya bade, yeh un reasons mein se ek tha kyunki yeh fail raha, lekin ek doosra aur behtar kaaran bhi tha. Agar Judge sirf bare assertion (sirf kehne) par ruk jaate, toh iska ek achha khasa asar hota; lekin unhone apni position ko prove karne ki koshish karne ki galti ki. Kuch saalon se Wilson personally apne manoranjan ke liye ek anokhe almanac (panchang) par kaam kar rahe the—ek calendar, jisme ek chhote se dikhne wale philosophy ka dab (saar) thha, jo aam taur par vyang-roop (ironical form) mein hota tha, jo har date ke sath joda (appended) gya tha; aur Judge ne socha ki Wilson ke yeh quips aur fancies (vyang aur kalpanayein) sateek roop se ghume hue aur cute hain; isliye woh ek din unmein se ek mutthi bhar lekar ghumme, aur unhein kuch mukhya citizens ko padh kar sunaya. Lekin vyang (irony) un logon ke liye nahi tha; unqi mansik drishti (mental vision) ispar focussed nahi thi. Unhone un playful trifles (khel-bhari mamuli cheezon) ko poori gombhirta (solidest earnest) mein padha, aur bina kisi hichkichahat ke faisala kiya ki agar kabhi is baare mein koi shakk tha ki Dave Wilson ek pudd’nhead hai—jo ki nahi tha—toh is khulase (revelation) ne us shakk ko hamesha ke liye door kar diya. Is duniya mein baseline yahi hai; ek enemy kisi mard ko aashik roop se barbaad kar sakta hai, lekin us cheez ko complete aur perfect banane ke liye ek good-natured bina-samajh dost (injudicious friend) ki zarurat hoti hai. Iske baad Judge Wilson ke prati pehle se kahin zyaada naram (tenderer) feel karne lage, aur pehle se kahin zyaada sure the ki unke calendar mein merit hai.

Judge Driscoll ek free-thinker ho sakte the aur tab bhi society mein apni jagah barkarar rakh sakte the kyunki woh community mein sabse bade mahatva ke insaan (person of most consequence) the, aur isliye apne khud ke raaste par jaane aur apne vichaaron ko follow karne ki dharstata kar sakte the. Unqi is pasandida organization ke doosre member ko wahi same liberty allowed thin kyunki woh public ke moolyankan mein ek shunya (cipher) the, aur koi bhi is baat ko koi importance nahi deta tha ki woh kya sochte hain ya karte hain. Unhein pasand kiya jata tha, woh har taraf kafi welcome the, lekin woh simply kisi cheez mein ginte nahi (didn’t count for anything) the.

Widow Cooper—jinhein har koi affection se “aunt Patsy” kehta tha—apni daughter Rowena ke sath ek comely cottage (khoobsurat ghar) mein rehti thin, jo nineteen saal ki thin, romantic, amiable (milansar), aur bahut pretty thin, lekin otherwise kisi mahatva ki nahi thin. Rowena ke paas ek-do young brothers the—woh bhi kisi mahatva ke nahi the.

Widow ke paas ek bada khali room (spare room) tha jise woh board (khane-peene) ke sath kisi lodger (kirayedar) ko rent par detin jab unhein koi mil pata, lekin yeh room unke dukh ke kaaran ab ek saal se khaali tha. Unqi income sirf family support ke liye paryapt thi, aur unhein choti luxuries (mamuli aaram) ke liye lodging-money ki zarurat thi. Lekin ab, aakhirkar, June ke ek garm din (flaming June day), unhone apne aap ko happy paaya; unka thaka dene wala wait khatam ho gya tha; unke saal bhar purane advertisement ka javab mil gya tha; aur kisi village ke applicant dwara nahi, oh, nahi!—yeh letter North mein sthit us dhundhle bade world se door se aaya tha: yeh St. Louis se tha. Woh apne porch par baith kar un dekhne wali aankhon (unseeing eyes) se mighty Mississippi ke chamkte hue daires (shining reaches) ko dekh rahi thin, unke vichaar unqi is achhi kismat (good fortune) mein doobe the. Indeed, yeh khhasakar achhi kismat thi, kyunki unhein ek ke bajaye do lodgers milne wale the.

Unhone family ko letter padh kar sunaya tha, aur Rowena slave aurat Nancy dwara room ki cleaning aur airing (hawa lagane) ko dekhne ke liye dance karti hui gayi thin, aur boys is badi news ko phhailane ke liye town mein baahar bhaage the, kyunki yeh public interest ka mamla tha, aur public hairan hoti aur khush nahi hoti agar unhein inform na kiya jata. Jaldi hi Rowena wapas aayin, khushi ke utsah se poori tarah lal (all ablush), aur letter ko dobara padhne (re-reading) ki guzarish ki. Yeh is tareeqe se framed tha:

> **HONORED MADAM:** *My brother and I have seen your advertisement, by chance, and beg leave to take the room you offer. We are twenty-four years of age and twins. We are Italians by birth, but have lived long in the various countries of Europe, and several years in the United States. Our names are Luigi and Angelo Capello. You desire but one guest; but dear Madam, if you will allow us to pay for two, we will not incommode you. We shall be down Thursday.*
> *(Aadarneeya Madam: Mere bhai aur maine sanyog se aapka advertisement dekha hai, aur aapke dwara offer kiye gaye room ko lene ki izazat chahte hain. Hum twenty-four saal ke hain aur judwa [twins] hain. Hum janm se Italian hain, lekin Europe ke tarah-tarah ke deshoon mein lambe samay tak rahe hain, aur kai saal United States mein. Hamare naam Luigi aur Angelo Capello hain. Aap sirf ek guest chahti hain; lekin priya Madam, agar aap hamein do logon ke liye pay karne ki izazat dengi, toh hum aapko koi asuvidha [incommode] nahi pahunchayenge. Hum Thursday ko neeche aayenge.)*

"Italians! Kitna romantic hai! Bas socho, ma—is town mein kabhi koi nahi aaya hai, aur har koi unhein dekhne ke liye mar raha hoga, aur woh poori tarah hamare hain! Us baare mein socho!"

"Haan, main sochti hoon woh ek bada stir (halchal) paada karenge."

"Oh, indeed woh karenge. Poora town apne head ke bal ho jayega! Socho—woh Europe aur har jagah rahe hain! Is town mein pehle kabhi koi traveler nahi aaya hai. Ma, main hairan nahi hoongi agar unhone kings ko dekha ho!"

"Well, koi bata nahi sakta, lekin woh uske bina bhi kafi stir paada karenge."

"Haan, woh toh o' course hai. Luigi—Angelo. Yeh lovely names hain; aur itne grand aur foreign hain—Jones aur Robinson aur un jaise nahi. Thursday ko woh aa rahe hain, aur yeh sirf Tuesday hai; wait karne ke liye yeh ek krrwa lamba samay (cruel long time) hai. Yahan gate ke andar Judge Driscoll aa rahe hain. Unhone is baare mein suna hai. Main jaungi aur door open karungi."

Judge congratulations aur jigyasa se bhare the. Letter ko padha aur discuss kiya gya. Jald hi Justice Robinson mazeed congratulations ke sath aaye, aur ek nayi reading aur ek naye discussion hua. Yeh shuruat thi. Neighbor ke baad neighbor, dono sexes ke, follow karte gaye, aur procession poore din aur evening aur poori Wednesday aur Thursday andar-baahar chalti rahi. Letter ko tab tak padha aur dobara padha gya jab tak ki yeh lagbhag phat (worn out) nahi gya; har kisi ne iske durbari aur gracious tone, aur smooth aur practised style ki tareef ki, har koi sympathetic aur excited tha, aur Coopers us poore samay khushi mein doobe the.

In purane samayon (primitive times) mein kam pani (low water) mein boats bahut uncertain thin. Is baar Thursday ki boat raat ke das baje tak nahi pahunchei thi—toh log poore din landing par be-fayda wait karte rahe; ek bhaari toofaan (heavy storm) dwara unhein unke gharon ki taraf dhakela gya bina un prabhavshali foreigners (illustrious foreigners) ka ek nazaara haasil kiye.

Gyaarah baje ka samay aaya; aur Cooper ka ghar town mein akela tha jisme abhi bhi lights jal rahi thin. Rain aur thunder abhi bhi goonj (booming) rahe the, aur chintit family abhi bhi wait kar rahi thi, abhi bhi hope kar rahi थी. Aakhirkar door par ek knock hua aur family ise open karne ke liye jump ki. Do negro mard enter hue, har ek ek trunk carry kiye hue, aur upstairs guest-room ki taraf badhe. Phir twins ne enter kiya—sabse handsome, sabse behtar kapde pehne, sabse vishisht dikhne wale (most distinguished-looking) young bandon ki jodi jise West ne kabhi dekha tha. Ek doosre se thoda fair tha, lekin otherwise woh exact duplicates the.

---

## The 9 Principles Checklist of Ultralearning

*(In-Context Strategy Alignment Review)*

Tom ke Yale se badlavon, Judge Driscoll ke arguments, aur judwa bhaion ke aagaman ko dekh kar, cognitive efficiency ke mutabik apni strategy checklist ko review karein:

* **[ ] 1. Metalearning (First Draw a Map):** Tom ne Yale ke curriculum ke mutabik "conditions" ka map taiyar kiya, bhale hi unka end goal structural competence haasil karna nahi tha.
* **[ ] 2. Focus (Sharpen Your Knife):** Tom ne shehri kapdo aur gloves ke bhatkaav (distraction) se town mein parade ki; public feedback ke karrwe-pan se seekh kar local fashion par switch kiya.
* **[ ] 3. Directness (Go Straight Ahead):** Wilson ke calendar ke vyang (irony) par citizens ka real-world response dikhata hai ki amurt concepts (abstract concepts) bina direct context ke gair-effective hote hain.
* **[ ] 4. Drill (Attack Your Weakest Point):** Judge Driscoll ne Wilson ke calendar ko sabko padha kar uski positioning ko prove karne ka prayas kiya; subcomponents ko bina sachet vishleshan ke bahaar nikaalna backfire kar sakta hai.
* **[ ] 5. Retrieval (Test to Learn):** Widow Cooper ne saal bhar purane advertisement ke response ko baar-baar padha aur check kiya, jo jankari ko dimaag mein securely store karne ka continuous review process hai.

---

# Chapter VI — Swimming in Glory

### *(Gaurav Ke Sagar Mein Tairna)*

---

> *Let us endeavor so to live that when we come to die even the undertaker will be sorry.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Hamein is tarah jeene ka prayas karna chahiye ki jab hamari maut aaye, toh kafan-dafan karne wala [undertaker] bhi dukh jatae.)*
> *Habit is habit, and not to be flung out of the window by any man, but coaxed down-stairs a step at a time.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Aadat toh aadat hai, jise koi bhi insaan khidki se baahar nahi phenk sakta, balki use dhere-dhere ek-ek kadam karke neeche utarna padta hai.)*

---

Subah breakfast ke dauran, judwa bhaion ke bolne ke aakarshak tareeqe (charm of manner) aur unke aasan aur polished bearing ne family ke dil ko jaldi se jeet (conquest) liya. Saari jhijhak aur formality jaldi se ghaayab ho gayi, aur uski jagah sabse dostana bhavna (friendliest feeling) aa gayi. Aunt Patsy unhein shuruat se hi unke Christian names se pukaarne lagin. Woh unke baare mein sabse teez jigyasa (keenest curiosity) se bhari thin, aur unhone ise dikhaya; bhaion ne apne baare mein baatcheet karke response diya, jisne unhein bahut khush kiya. Jaldi hi yeh zahir hua ki apni early youth mein unhone gareebi aur mushqil (poverty and hardship) dekhi thi. Jaise-jaise baatcheet aage bhatki (wandered along), purani lady us mamle ke baare mein ek-do sawaal daalane ke liye sahi jagah ki taak mein rahin, aur jab unhein yeh mili toh unhone blond twin (gore judwa bhai) se kaha, jo ab brunette (sawnle) bhai ke aaram karne ke dauran apni biography batane ki apni baari kar raha thha—

“Mr. Angelo, agar yeh aisa sawaal na ho jo mujhe nahi poochna chahiye, toh jab aap chote the toh aap itne sahara-heen (friendless) aur trouble mein kaise aaye? Kya aapko batane mein koi parwah hai? Lekin agar hai toh mat bataiye.”

“Oh, hamein is baare mein bilkul koi parwah nahi hai, madam; hamare case mein yeh merely ek badkismat (misfortune) thi, aur kisi ki galti nahi thi. Hamare parents Italy mein acche-khase ameer (well to do) the, aur hum unqi akeli bacha the. Hum purane Florentine kulinata (nobility) se the”—Rowena ka dil ek vishal udaan bhara, unki naak phhaili, aur unqi aankhon mein ek fine roshni kheli—“aur jab war shuru hui toh mere father haarne wali side par the aur unhein apni life bachane ke liye bhaagna pada. Unqi jameen (estates) confiscate kar li gayi, unqi personal property zapt (seized) ho gayi, aur hum wahan Germany mein strangers, friendless, aur actually paupers (kangal) the. Mera bhai aur main ten saal ke the, aur us umra ke hisab se well-educated (padhe-likhe) the, bahut studious (padhaku), kitabhon ke shaukeen, aur German, French, Spanish, aur English bhashon mein hamara aadhar mazboot (well grounded) tha. Sath hi, hum adbhut musical prodigies (vilakshan sangheet pratibha) the—agar aap mujhe aisa kehne ki izazat dein, kyunki yeh sirf sach hai.

“Hamare father apni badkismaton ke baad sirf ek mahina hi zinda rahe, hamari mother jaldi hi unke piche chali gayin, aur hum duniya mein akele the. Hamare parents hamein ek tamashe (show) ke roop mein pradarshit karke khud ko comfortable bana sakte the, aur unhein kai bade offers mile the; lekin us vichaar ne unke garv ko na-pasand (revolted) kar diya, aur unhone kaha ki woh pehle bhookhe mar jayenge. Lekin jis cheez ke liye woh razi nahi hue, woh hamein bina kisi kanooni sahamati (formality of consent) ke karna pada. Unqi bimari aur unke janaze (funerals) ke kaaran hue karz ke badle hamein zapt (seized) kar liya gya, aur karz chukane ke paise (liquidation money) kamane ke liye Berlin ke ek saste museum ke attractions ke beech rakh diya gya. Us slavery se baahar nikalne mein hamein do saal lage. Hum bina kisi mazdoori (wages) ke, aur yahan tak ki khane-peene ke bina poore Germany mein travel karte rahe. Hamein bina kisi cheez ke pradarshit (exhibited) kiya jata, aur apni roti mangni padti thi.

“Well, madam, baaki ka hissa bahut zyaada mahatva ka nahi hai. Jab hum twelve saal ki umra mein us slavery se bhaage, toh hum kuch mayno mein mard (men) ban chuke the. Experience ne hamein kuch keemti cheezein sikha di thin; doosron ke beech, apna khhayal kaise rakhna hai, sharks aur dhokebaazon (sharpers) se kaise bachna aur unhein harana hai, aur bina doosre logon ki madad ke apne khud ke profit ke liye apna khud ka business kaise chalana (conduct) hai. Hum har jagah ghumme—saalon aur saalon tak—anandit bhashon ki thodi-thodi jankari (smatterings of strange tongues) ikhatha karte hue, ajeeb nazaaron aur ajeeb customs se khud ko familiar karte hue, ek wide, vaividhya-purna aur jigyasa-bhari (curious) tarah ki shiksha ikhatha karte hue. Yeh ek pleasant life thi. Hum Venice gaye—London, Paris, Russia, India, China, Japan—”

Is point par Nancy, slave aurat ne door par apna head andar dhakela aur chilla uthi:

“Ole Missus, ghar logon se plum’ jam full (khacha-khach bhara) hai, aur woh in gentlemen ko dekhne ke liye bilkul tadap (jes aspi’lin’) rahe hain!” Unhone apne head ke ek ishare (nod) se judwa bhaion ki taraf sanket kiya, aur ise wapas nazar se door chhupa liya.

Yeh widow ke liye ek garv ka mauqa (proud occasion) tha, aur unhone apne neighbors aur doston ke samne apne in fine foreign birds ko show off karne mein bade santoosh ka vaada kiya—sadharan log (simple folk) jinhone mushkil se kabhi kisi tarah ke foreigner ko dekha tha, aur vishishtata ya style (distinction or style) wale ko toh kabhi nahi. Phir bhi unqi feeling Rowena ke comparison mein nishchit roop se kamzor thi. Rowena baadlon (clouds) mein thin, woh hawa mein chalti thin; yeh us dull country town ki be-rang history mein sabse bada din, sabse romantic episode hone wala tha. Woh iski gaurav (glory) ke srot ke paas parichay se rehne wali thin aur iske poore flood (pravah) ko apne upar aur apne chaaron taraf undelte hue feel karne wali thin; doosri girls sirf dekh saktin aur jalan kar saktin thin, part nahi le saktin thin.

Widow ready thin, Rowena ready thin, aur foreign bhaion bhi ready the. Party hall ke sath aige badhi, judwa bhaion aage the, aur parlor ke khule door mein enter kiya, jahan se baatcheet ki ek halki goonj (low hum) nikal rahi thi. Judwa bhaion ne door ke paas ek position li, widow Luigi ke side khadi thin, Rowena Angelo ke paas khadi thin, aur march-past aur introductions shuru hue. Widow poori tarah smiles aur santoosh se bhari thin. Unhone procession ko receive kiya aur ise Rowena ke sahare pass kiya.

“Good mornin’, Sister Cooper”—hand-shake.

“Good morning, Brother Higgins—Count Luigi Capello, Mr. Higgins”—hand-shake, jiske baad Higgins ki taraf se ek bhookhi ghoorthi hui nazar (devouring stare) aur “Aapise milkar glad hoon” aaya, aur Count Luigi ki taraf se head ka ek shishtata-bhara jhukaav (courteous inclination) aur ek pleasant “Most happy!” aaya.

“Good mornin’, Roweny”—hand-shake.

“Good morning, Mr. Higgins—aapko Count Angelo Capello se present karti hoon.”

Hand-shake, adbhut ghoorthi hui nazar, “Glad to see ye,”—courteous nod, smily “Most happy!” aur Higgins aage badh jaata hai.

In visitors mein se koi bhi comfortable (at ease) nahi tha, lekin, honest log hone ke naate, unhone aisa hone ka pretend nahi kiya. Unmein se kisi ne pehle kabhi kulinata ka title (title of nobility) rakhne wale kisi insaan ko nahi dekha tha, aur koi bhi abhi aishi umeed nahi kar raha tha, nateejatan title unpar ek khambha-gaadne wale surprise (pile-driving surprise) ki tarah aaya aur unhein bina taiyari ke pakad (caught them unprepared) liya. Kuch ne emergency ke hisab se uthne ki koshish ki, aur ek anadi “My lord,” ya “Your lordship,” ya us tarah ka kuch nikaala, lekin badi sankya (great majority) us asamanya sabd aur chamkte hue durbari (gilded courts), shandaar ceremony aur pavitra raj-pad (anointed kingship) ke sath iske dhundhle aur awful associations se poori tarah dab (overwhelmed) gayi thi, isliye unhone sirf hand-shake mein her-pher kiya aur bina lafzon ke aage badh gaye.

Kabhi-kabar, jaisa har jagah saari receptions mein hota hai, ek samanya se zyaada dostana aatma (ordinary friendly soul) ne procession ko block kar diya aur ise wait karne par majboor rakkha jabki unhone inquiry ki ki bhaion ko village kaisa laga, aur woh kab tak rukne wale hain, aur kya unqi families well hain, aur weather ko beech mein kheench laye, aur hope ki ki yeh jaldi hi cooler ho jayega, aur us tarah ki saari cheezein, taaki jab woh ghar pahunchein toh yeh kehne kabil hon, “Maine unke sath kaafi lambi talk ki thi”; lekin kisi ne koi pachhtave jaisi cheez nahi ki ya kahi, aur is tarah yeh bada mamla (great affair) ek vishwasniya aur santoshjanak tareeqe (creditable and satisfactory fashion) se ant tak poora hua.

General conversation follow hui, aur judwa bhaion ek group se doosre group mein chaaron taraf drift hote gaye, aasaani aur faraatedar tareeqe (easily and fluently) se baatcheet karte hue aur sahamati (approval) jeet-te hue, admiration par majboor karte hue aur sabse favor haasil karte hue. Widow ne ek garv-bhari eye ke sath unqi is jeetne wali march (conquering march) ko follow kiya, aur har kuch samay baad Rowena ne gehri santushti ke sath apne aap se kaha, “Aur yeh sochna ki woh hamare hain—poori tarah hamare!”

Mother ya daughter ke liye koi bekar moments (idle moments) nahi the. Judwa bhaion ke baare mein utsaahit inquiries poore samay unke jaadui kaano (enchanted ears) mein undeli ja rahi thin; har ek saas-roke sunne walon (breathless listeners) ke ek group ka constant center thi; har ek ne recognize kiya ki woh ab pehli baar us bade sabd **Gaurav (Glory)** ka asli matlab jaanti hai, aur iski vishal keemat (stupendous value) ko perceive karti hai, aur samajhti hai ki kyun har daur mein mard iski shreshth aur charam joy (sublime and supreme joy) ka ek taste paane ke liye mamuli khushiyon, khazane, aur khud life ko phenkne ke liye taiyar rahe hain. Napoleon aur unke jaise saarre logon ka hisab mil gya tha—aur sahi thehrana (justified) gya tha.

Jab Rowena ne aakhirkar parlor mein logon ke prati apni saari duty poori kar li, toh woh upstairs ek overflow-meeting (baahar tak bhari meeting) ki ichhaon ko santusht karne ke liye gayin, kyunki parlor saare aane walon ko hold karne ke liye bada nahi tha. Ek baar phir unhein utsaahit sawaal karne walon (eager questioners) dwara gher (besieged) liya gya aur ek baar phir woh gaurav ke sunset seas (sunset seas of glory) mein tairne lagin. Jab dopahar (forenoon) lagbhag chali gayi, toh unhone ek gehre dard (pang) ke sath recognize kiya ki unqi life ka yeh sabse shandaar episode lagbhag khatam ho gya hai, ki koi cheez ise lamba nahi khinch sakti, ki iske barabar ka kuch bhi unqi kismat mein kabhi dobara nahi aane wala hai. Lekin parwah nahi, yeh apne aap mein paryapt (sufficient unto itself) tha, grand mauqa shuruat se hi ek badhte hue paimane (ascending scale) par aage badha tha, aur ek umda aur yaadgar success tha. Agar judwa bhaion ab ise climax dene ke liye koi bada act (crowning act) kar sakein, kuch unusual, kuch startling, company ke sabse oonche admiration ko apne upar concentrate karne ke liye kuch, ek electric surprise ke nature mein kuch—

Yahan neeche ek vishal slam-banging (bhat-bhatahat) shuru hui, aur har koi dekhne ke liye neeche bhaaga. Yeh judwa bhaion piano par bade style mein ek classic four-handed piece (char haathon wala sangheet) nikaal rahe the. Rowena satisfied thin—apne dil ke bottom tak satisfied thin.

Young strangers ko lambe samay tak piano par rakkha gya. Villagers unqi performance ke mahatva par hairan aur jaaduit (astonished and enchanted) the, aur unke rukne ko bardaasht nahi kar sakte the. Jo bhi music unhone pehle kabhi suna tha, woh is sur-mili awaaz ke nasha dene wale floods (intoxicating floods of melodious sound) ke comparison mein bina-atma ka nau-sikhia kaam (spirites prentice-work) aur grace ya charm se khaali lagta tha. Unhone realize kiya ki unqi life mein ek baar ke liye woh **masters (gurus)** ko sun rahe the.

---

## The 9 Principles Checklist of Ultralearning

*(In-Context Strategy Alignment Review)*

Judwa bhaion ke asadharn talent aur public response ko moolyankan karte hue, skill mastery ke principles ke mutabik apni strategy checklist ko review karne ka abhyas karein:

* **[ ] 1. Metalearning (First Draw a Map):** Judwa bhaion ne bataya ki 10 saal ki umra mein hi unka German, French, Spanish, aur English bhashon ka aadhar mazboot (well grounded) tha, jo early age mein structured linguistic mapping ka perfect example hai.
* **[ ] 2. Focus (Sharpen Your Knife):** Rowena gaurav ke ghoonghat (clouds of glory) mein bina bhatke poore din aur evening check-ins par focus rahi; public validation ke asar mein apna attention mukhya event par rakkha.
* **[ ] 3. Directness (Go Straight Ahead):** Bhaion ne 12 saal ki umra mein slavery se bhaag kar directly real-world mein "sharks aur dhokebaazon" se deal karna seekha; pratyaksh anubhav (direct experience) hi unqi survival skill ka backbone bana.
* **[ ] 4. Drill (Attack Your Weakest Point):** Higgins aur doosre village ke log "My Lord" jaise kulinata ke naye sabdon ko pukaarne mein ladkhadaye (fumbled); jab context nayan ho, toh subcomponents par alag se drill karna zaruri ho jata hai.
* **[ ] 5. Retrieval (Test to Learn):** Bhaion ne bachpan se seekhi bhashon aur musical chords ka bina kisi material ke public parlor mein direct pradarshan kiya, jo memory se deep representations ko successfully retrieve karne ka performance vector hai.
* **[ ] 6. Feedback (Don’t Dodge the Punches):** Audience ke chehron ki hairani aur live chatter se bhaion ko moment-to-moment informational feedback mil raha tha, jise unhone piano par aur behtar performance dene ke liye use kiya.
* **[ ] 7. Retention (Don’t Fill a Leaky Bucket):** Bhaion ka saalon tak alag-alag deshoon (India, China, Japan) mein ghoomte hue bhashon ko use karna spacing niyan ko pradarshit karta hai, jisse unka knowledge kabhi leak nahi hua.
* **[ ] 8. Intuition (Dig Deep Before Building Up):** Villagers ne realize kiya ki woh "masters" ko sun rahe hain; bhaion ka piano par bina soche sateek chords bajana long-term memory mein stored 50,000 dimaagi "chunks" ke intuitive execution ko dikhata hai.
* **[ ] 9. Experimentation (Explore Outside Your Comfort Zone):** Bhaion ne simple piano piece ke bajaye ek "classic four-handed electric surprise" try kiya; comfort zone se baahar badh kar kiya gya yeh extreme prayog hi unqi gauravshali safalata ka mukhya kaaran bana.

---

# Chapter VII — The Unknown Nymph

### *(Ajanabi Sundari)*

---

> *One of the most striking differences between a cat and a lie is that a cat has only nine lives.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Ek cat aur ek jhooth [lie] ke beech sabse bada farq yeh hai ki cat ke paas sirf nau lives hoti hain.)*

---

Mahfil reluctantly (bina man ke) khatam hui, aur log apne-apne gharon ki taraf chal pade, vivacity (purn utsah) ke sath baatcheet karte hue aur is baat par sahmat hote hue ki Dawson’s Landing mein is jaisa bada din dobara dekhne mein abhi kai din lagenge. Jab reception chal rahi thi tabhi judwa bhaion ne kai invitations sweekar kar liye the, aur unhone ek local charity (sthaniya daan) ke labh ke liye ek amateur entertainment (shaukia manoranjan) mein kuch duets (jugalbandi) bajane ke liye khud ko volunteer (pesh) bhi kiya tha. Society unhein apne gale lagane (receive to its bosom) ke liye utsaahit thi. Judge Driscoll ke paas unhein turant ek drive par le jaane aur unhein sabse pehle public mein display karne ka good fortune (achha bhagya) tha. Woh unki buggy mein unke sath enter hue, aur mukhya sarak par unki parade nikaali gayi, jise dekhne ke liye har koi windows aur sidewalks par ikhatha ho gya.

Judge ne un strangers ko naya qabristan (graveyard), aur jail, aur shehar ka sabse ameer mard kahan rehta hai, aur Freemasons’ hall, aur Methodist church, aur Presbyterian church, aur Baptist church kahan banne wali hai jab unhein iske nirman ke liye kuch paise mil jayenge, yeh sab dikhaya, aur unhein town hall aur slaughter-house (kasai-khana) bhi dikhaya, aur uniform pehne swatantra fire company ko baahar nikaala aur unse ek kaalpnik aag (imaginary fire) bujhwai; phir unhone unhein militia company ki muskets (bandookein) jaanchne di, aur in saari shandariyon par utsah ka ek exhaustless stream (khatam na hone wala pravah) undel diya, aur unhein jo responses mile unse woh bahut zyaada satisfied dikhe, kyunki judwa bhaion ne unke us admiration ko saraaha (admired), aur jitna behtar woh kar sakte the unhein badla chukaya, halanki woh isse mazeed behtar kar sakte the agar alag-alag deshoon mein is tarah ke lagbhag pandrah ya solah lakh pehle ke experiences ne pehle se hi iske naveenta (novelty) ke ek bade hisse ko mita na diya hota.

Judge ne unhein ek achha samay bitane ke liye hosptably (mehmaan-nawazi se) poori jaan laga di, aur agar kahin koi kami (defect) thi toh woh unki galti nahi thi. Unhone unhein kai humorous anecdotes (mazaak-bhari kahaniyan) sunayin, aur hamesha mukhya nuktah (nub) bhool jaate the, lekin bhaion hamesha use provide karne kabil the, kyunki yeh kahaniyan kaafi purane zamane ki thin, aur unhone pehle bhi kai baar unpar tazgi-bhara haath azmaya tha. Aur unhone unhein apni tarah-tarah ki daddvtaon (dignities) ke baare mein sab kuch bataya, aur kaise unhone samman ya labh ke is aur us aur doosre sthanon ko hold kiya tha, aur ek baar legislature (vidhan-sabha) mein bhi gaye the, aur ab *Society of Free-thinkers* ke president the. Unhone kaha ki society char saal se exist kar rahi hai, aur iske paas pehle se hi do members hain, aur yeh firmly establish ho chuki hai. Woh evening mein bhaion ke paas aayenge agar woh iski ek meeting attend karna chahein.

Accordingly (Iske mutabik) woh unhein lene aaye, aur raaste mein unhone unhein Pudd’nhead Wilson ke baare mein sab kuch bataya, taaki unhein pehle se hi unke baare mein ek favorable impression mil sake aur unhein pasand karne ke liye taiyar reh sakein. Yeh yojana safal rahi—favorable impression haasil ho gya. Baad mein iski confirmation tab hui aur yeh solidified ho gya jab Wilson ne prastav rakkha (proposed) ki strangers ke prati shishtatar (courtesy) ke roop mein usual topics ko ek taraf rakh diya jaye aur ghante ko sadharan subjects (ordinary subjects) par baatcheet aur dostana rishton aur acche saathi-pan (good-fellowship) ko badhava dene ke liye devot kiya jaye,—ek aisa prastav jise vote ke liye rakkha gya aur pass (carried) kar diya gya.

Ghanta teez talk mein jaldi se guzar gya, aur jab yeh khatam hua toh lonesome aur neglected Wilson usse kahin zyaada ameer the do doston se jitne woh tab the jab yeh shuru hua tha. Unhone twins ko jaldi hi unke lodgings (kamre) par aane ka invite kiya, ek beech ke engagement ko niptaane ke baad, aur unhone khushi ke sath sweekar kiya.

Evening ke beech ke paas unhone apne aap ko unke ghar ke raaste par paaya. Pudd’nhead ghar par unka wait kar rahe the aur apna samay ek aishi cheez par puzzle karne (sochne) mein laga rahe the jo us subah unqi nazar mein aayi thi. Mamla yeh tha: Woh sanyog se bahut jaldi uth gaye the—actually bhor (dawn) ke samay; aur unhone us hall ko cross kiya jo unke cottage ko center se divide karta tha, aur wahan se kuch lene ke liye ek room mein enter hue. Room ki khidki par koi curtains nahi the, kyunki ghar ka woh side lambe samay se unoccupied (khali) tha, aur is khidki se unqi nazar ek aishi cheez par padi jisne unhein surprises aur interested kiya. Yeh ek young woman thi—ek young woman jahan properly kisi young woman ka koi talluk nahi tha; kyunki woh Judge Driscoll ke ghar mein thin, aur Judge ke private study ya sitting-room ke upar wale bedroom mein thin. Yeh young Tom Driscoll ka bedroom tha. Woh aur Judge, Judge ki vidhwa sister Mrs. Pratt aur teen negro servants akela log the jo us ghar se belong karte the. Phir, yeh young lady kaun ho sakti hai? Donho ghar ek sadharan aangan (ordinary yard) se alag the, jiske beech mein samne sarak se lekar piche ki gali tak ek kam-oonchi fence chalti thi. Doori bahut zyaada nahi thi, aur Wilson ladki ko kaafi achhi tarah dekhne kabil the, kyunki woh jis room mein thin uske window-shades upar the, aur khidki bhi. Ladki ne ek neat aur trim summer dress pehni thi, jo pink aur white rang ke bade patti-dar patterns (broad stripes) mein thi, aur unqi bonnet par ek pink veil (ghoonghat) laga tha. Woh apparently steps, gaits (chalne ka dhang) aur attitudes ka abhyas (practising) kar rahi thin; woh is cheez ko gracefully kar rahi thin, aur apne kaam mein bahut zyaada absorbed thin. Woh kaun ho sakti thi, aur woh young Tom Driscoll ke room mein kaise aayi thi?

Wilson ne jaldi se ek aishi position chun li thi jahan se woh unqi taraf se dekhe jaane ke bade risk ke bina ladki ko watch kar sakein, aur woh wahin rahe is hope mein ki woh apna veil uthayegi aur apna face zahir (betray) karegi. Lekin usne unhein disappoint kiya. Lagbhag twenty minutes ke mamle ke baad woh ghaayab ho gayi, aur bhale hi woh aadhe ghante mazeed tak apni post par rahe, woh dobara nahi aayi.

Dopahar ke paas woh Judge ke yahan drop in (aaye) aur Mrs. Pratt se din ke bade event ke baare mein baat ki, Aunt Patsy Cooper ke yahan prabhavshali foreigners ke levee (sammelan) ke baare mein. Unhone unke nephew Tom ke baare mein poocha, aur unhone kaha ki woh ghar aane ke raaste par hain, aur woh expect kar rahi hain ki woh raat se thoda pehle arrive honge; aur add kiya ki woh aur Judge is baat se gratified (khush) hain unke letters se yeh jankari ikhatha karke ki woh apna vyavahar bahut nicely aur creditably (sarishtata se) chala rahe hain—jispar Wilson ne secretly apne aap se wink (aankh maari) kiya. Wilson ne yeh nahi poocha ki kya ghar mein koi naya newcomer aaya hai, lekin unhone aise sawaal pooche jinhone us mamle ke baare mein light-throwing answers (roshni dalne wale javab) nikaale hote agar Mrs. Pratt ke paas daalane ke liye koi roshni hoti; isliye woh yeh satisfied hokar chale gaye ki woh unke ghar mein chal rahi un cheezon ke baare mein jaante the jisse woh khud anjaan (not aware) thin.

Woh ab twins ka wait kar rahe the, aur abhi bhi is problem par puzzle kar rahe the ki woh girl kaun ho sakti hai, aur woh us young bande ke room mein subah bhor ke samay (at daybreak) kaise majood thi.
---

# Chapter VIII — Marse Tom Tramples His Chance

### *(Marse Tom Apne Mauqe Ko Kuchtal Deta Hai)*

---

> *The holy passion of Friendship is of so sweet and steady and loyal and enduring a nature that it will last through a whole lifetime, if not asked to lend money.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Dosti [Friendship] ka pavitra jazba itna meetha, sthir, vafadar aur tikau hota hai ki yeh poori life chal sakta hai, bhasharte isse paise udhaar mangne ke liye na kaha jaye.)*
> *Consider well the proportions of things. It is better to be a young June-bug than an old bird of paradise.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Cheezon ke anupaat [proportions] par achhi tarah vichar karein. Ek boodhe bird of paradise hone se behtar hai ek young June-bug banna.)*

---

Ab Roxy ko dhoondhna (hunt up) zaroori hai.

Jis samay unhein free kiya gya aur woh chambermaiding par gayin, woh thirty-five saal ki thin. Unhein New Orleans ke vyapar mein chalne wali ek Cincinnati boat, *Grand Mogul*, par second chambermaid ke roop mein ek berth (naukri) mili. Ek-do trips ne unhein kaam ka aadi (wonted) aur easy-going bana diya, aur steamboat life ke us stir (halchal), adventure aur independence ne unhein poori tarah se jaaduit (infatuated) kar diya. Phir unqi promotion hui aur woh head chambermaid ban gayin. Woh officers ki favorite thin, aur unke mazaak-bhare aur dostana tareeqon par tezi se proud thin.

Aath saal tak unhone saal ke teen hisse us boat par serve kiya, aur winters ek Vicksburg packet par bitaye. Lekin ab do mahine se unke haathon mein gathiya (rheumatism) tha, aur unhein kapde dhone ke tub (wash-tub) ko akele chhodne par majboor hona pada. So, unhone isteefa (resigned) de diya. Lekin woh well-fixed thin—rich (ameer), jaisa woh ise describe kartiin; kyunki unhone ek sthir life jiyi thi, aur apni old age ke prabandh ke roop mein har mahine New Orleans mein char dollars bank mein jama (banked) kiye the. Unhone shuruat mein kaha tha ki unhone “ek nange-pair nigger (bar'footed nigger) ko pehne ke liye jootey diye the taaki woh unpar hi kuchtal (tromple) sake,” aur aishi ek galti kafi thi; woh tab se hamesha ke liye insani race se independent ho jayengi agar hard work aur economy (bachat) ise accomplish kar sakein. Jab boat ne New Orleans mein levee (ghat) ko chhua toh unhone *Grand Mogul* par apne doston ko good-by kaha aur apna saaman (kit) kinare utar liya.

Lekin woh ek ghante mein wapas thin. Bank collapse (smash) ho gya tha aur unke char sau dollars (four hundred dollars) apne sath lekar chala gya tha. Woh ek pauper (kangal) thin, aur homeless. Sath hi sharir se apang (disabled), kam se kam filhal ke liye. Officers unqi is trouble mein poori tarah se sympathy se bhare the, aur unhone unke liye ek choti purse (paise) ikhatha ki. Unhone apne birthplace jaane ka nishchay kiya; negroes ke beech wahan unke dost the, aur badkismat hamesha badkismat ki madad karta hai, woh is baare mein achhi tarah aware thin; unqi youth ke woh mamuli saathi unhein bhookhe nahi marne denge.

Unhone Cairo mein choti local packet li, aur ab woh ghar ki aakhiri ddaud (home-stretch) par thin. Samay ne apne bete ke khilaf unqi karrwahat (bitterness) ko mita diya tha, aur woh unke baare mein shanti se sochne kabil thin. Unhone uske ghatiya side (vile side) ko apne mind se baahar nikaal diya, aur kevel unke prati uske kabhi-kabar ke kindness ke acts ki yaadon par tikin. Unhone unhein sringaarit (gilded/decorated) kiya, aur moolyankan karne ke liye unhein bahut pleasant banaya. Woh use dekhne ke liye tarasne (long to see him) lagin. Woh ek gulam ki tarah (slave-like) jaakar uspar apna pyaar jatayengi—kyunki nishchit roop se yahi unka posture hona tha—aur shayad woh payengi ki samay ne use badal (modified) diya hai, aur woh apni lambi-bhooli purani nurse ko dekh kar glad hoga aur uske sath gently treat karega. Yeh lovely hoga; yeh unhein unke dukhon (woes) aur unqi gareebi ko bhoolne par majboor kar dega.

Unqi gareebi! Us vichaar ne unhein apne dream mein ek aur qila (castle) add karne ke liye inspire kiya: shayad woh unhein kabhi-kabar thoda sa paisa (trifle) de de—shayad mahine mein ek baar ek dollar, maan lijiye; aishi koi bhi choti cheez bahut zyaada madad karegi, oh, bahut zyaada.

Jab tak woh Dawson’s Landing pahunchein woh phir se apni purani self thin; unka udasi-pan (blues) chala gya tha, woh oonche utsah (high feather) mein thin. Woh nishchitta se gujara kar lengi; aise kai kitchens the jahan servants unke sath apna khana share karenge, aur unke ghar le jaane ke liye sugar, apples aur doosre pakwan (dainties) bhi churayenge—ya unhein khud unhein churane (pilfer) ka ek chance denge, jo utna hi kaam karega. Aur wahan church tha. Woh pehle se kahin zyaada ek tivra aur samarpit (rabid and devoted) Methodist thin, aur unqi dharmikta koi dhokha (sham) nahi thi, balki strong aur sincere thi. Haan, dheron suvidhaon (creature comforts) aur amen-corner mein apni purani jagah dobara apne kabze mein hone ke sath, woh tab se ant tak poori tarah se happy aur shanti mein rahengi.

Woh sabse pehle Judge Driscoll ke kitchen mein gayin. Wahan unka swagat bade roop mein aur vishal utsah (vast enthusiasm) ke sath kiya gya. Unqi adbhut yatrayen, aur unke dwara dekhe gaye naye deshoon aur unke carnamo ne unhein ek achambha (marvel), aur romance ki ek heroine bana diya. Negroes unqi experiences ki badi kahani par jaaduit hokar latak gaye, utsaahit sawaalon, hansi, khushi ke chillane aur taaliyon ke pradarshano ke sath poore raaste unhein interrupt karte hue; aur woh apne aap se sweekar karne par majboor thin ki agar is duniya mein steamboating se behtar kuch tha, toh woh iske baare mein batane se haasil hone wala gaurav (glory) tha. Audience ne unke stomach ko apne dinners se bhar diya, aur phir unke basket ko bharne ke liye pantry ko poori tarah se saaf chura (stole bare) liya.

Tom St. Louis mein the. Servants ne bataya ki unhone pichele do saalon ke dauran apne samay ka sabse behtar hissa wahin spent kiya hai. Roxy daily aati thin, aur family aur iske mamlon ke baare mein kai talks kartin. Ek baar unhone poocha ki Tom itna baahar kyun rehta hai. Dikhne wale “Chambers” ne kaha:

“Fact yeh hai, jab young master shehar se baahar hota hai toh ole master mazeed behtar gujara kar sakte hain mukable iske jab woh shehar mein ho; haanh, aur woh use behtar pyaar bhi karte hain; isliye woh use fifty dollars a month dete hain—”

“Nahi, kya aisa hai? Chambers, tum mazaak kar rahe ho, hai na?”

“Sach keh raha hoon main nahi kar raha, mammy; Marse Tom ne mujhe khud aisa bataya tha. Lekin parwah nahi, yeh kafi nahi hai.”

“My lan’, kya kaaran hai ki yeh kafi nahi hai?”

“Well, main tumhein batane wala hoon, agar tum mujhe ek chance (chanst) do, mammy. Kaaran yeh kafi nahi hai kyunki Marse Tom gamble (jua) khelte hain.”

Roxy ne hairani (astonishment) mein apne haath upar uthaye aur Chambers jaatri raha—

“Ole master ne yeh figure out kar liya, kyunki unhein Marse Tom ke juye ke karz (gamblin' debts) ke liye do sau dollars (two hundred dollars) pay karne pade, aur yeh sach hai, mammy, theek utna hi nishchit jitna tum paada hui ho.”

“Do—sau—dollars! Arre, tum kis baare mein baat kar rahe ho? Do—sau—dollars. Baap re, yeh ek kafi achha second-hand nigger kharidne ke liye lagbhag paryapt hai. Aur tum jhooth nahi bol rahe ho, honey?—tum apni ole mammy se jhooth nahi bologe?”

“God ka apna sach hai, exactly jaisa main tumhein bata raha hoon—two hundred dollars—main prarthna karta hoon ki main apni jagah se kabhi na hiloon agar aisa na ho. Aur, oh, my lan’, ole Marse toh gusse mein kood rahe the! Woh ubalte hue gusse (b'ilin' mad) mein the, main tumhein batata hoon! Unhone use be-dakhal (dissenhurrit) kar diya.”

Us shandaar sabd (stately word) ke baad usne swad ke sath apne hont chaate (licked his chops). Roxy ne ek moment tak is sabd ke sath struggle kiya, phir ise chhod diya aur kaha—

“Dissen-kya kar diya?”

“Dissenhurrit (Disinherited - vasiyat se be-dakhal) kar diya.”

“Yeh kya hai? Iska matlab kya hai?”

“Matlab unhone vasiyat tod di (bu'sted de will).”

“Vasi-yat tod di! Groh use kabhi aise treat nahi karenge! Ise wapas lo, tum badkismat nakli nigger (mis'able imitation nigger) jise maine dukh aur peeda (sorrow en tribbilation) mein paada kiya.”

Roxy ka pasandida qila (pet castle)—Tom ki pocket se kabhi-kabar milne wala ek dollar—unqi aankhon ke samne barbaadi mein gir raha tha. Woh aise ek disaster ko bardaasht nahi kar saktin thin; woh is vichaar ko jhel nahi saktin thin. Unqi tippani ne Chambers ka manoranjan kiya:

“Yah-yah-yah! Bas use suno! Kaash main imitation hoon, toh aap kya hain? Hum dono nakli white (imitation white) hain—wahi hum hain—aur bahut acche nakli bhi—yah-yah-yah!—hum nakli negroes ke roop mein kisi ginti mein nahi aate; aur jahan tak—”

“Apni yeh bewakoofi band karo (Shet up yo' foolin'), isse pehle ki main tumhare head ke side par maroon, aur mujhe vasiyat ke baare mein batao. Mujhe batao ki yeh tooti nahi hai—batao, honey, aur main tumhein kabhi nahi bhoolungi.”

“Well, nahi tooti hai—kyunki ek nayi vasiyat banayi gayi hai, aur Marse Tom dobara perfectly alright hain. Lekin tum is baare mein itne pasine (sich a sweat) mein kyun ho, mammy? Mujhe nahi lagta ki yeh aapka koi business hai.”

“Yeh mera koi business nahi hai? Kiska business hai phir, main jaan'na chahungi? Kya main fifteen saal ke hone tak uski mother thin, ya nahi thin?—tum mujhe iska javab do. Aur tum expect karte ho ki main use duniya mein poor aur bekar turned out hote hue dekhoon aur is baare mein kabhi kuch care na karoon? Main sochti hoon agar tum kabhi khud ek mother rahe hote, Valet de Chambers, toh tum aishi bewakoofi ki baat nahi karte.”

“Well, toh, ole Marse ne unhein forgive kar diya aur vasiyat dobara fix up kar di—kya yeh aapko satisfy karta hai?”

Haan, woh ab satisfied thin, aur ispar kaafi happy aur bhavuk (sentimental) thin. Woh daily aati rahin, aur aakhirkar unhein bataya gya ki Tom ghar aa chuka hai. Woh utsah se kaanpne (tremble with emotion) lagin, aur turant yeh bheekh mangne ke liye sandesh bheja ki unke “poor ole nigger mammy ko unka sirf ek nazaara haasil karne dein aur khushi se mar jaane dein.”

Tom ek sofa par apni aaram-dayak aalsi suvidha (lazy ease) mein phhaile the jab Chambers ne prarthna (petition) prastut ki. Samay ne unqi childhood ke is mamuli mazdoor (humble drudge) aur protector ke prati unqi purani nafrat (ancient detestation) ko badal nahi tha; yeh abhi bhi karrwi aur samjhauta na karne wali (bitter and uncompromising) thi. Woh baith gaye aur us young mard ke fair face par ek karrwi nazar (severe gaze) daali jiska naam woh anjaane mein use kar rahe the aur jiske family rights ka woh anand le rahe the. Unhone nazar tab tak barkarar rakkhi jab tak ki iska victim darr se satisfactorily peela (pallid with terror) nahi ho gya, phir unhone kaha—

“Uss purani aafat (old rip) ko mujhse kya kaam hai?”

Prarthna ko vinamra roop se dohraya gya.

“Tumhein kisne permission di ki yahan aao aur negroes ki samajik attentions se mujhe disturb karo?”

Tom uth khade hue the. Doosra young man ab saaf roop se kaanp (trembling) raha tha. Usne dekha ki kya aane wala hai, aur apne head ko ek taraf jhuka diya, aur ise protect karne ke liye apna left haath upar utha liya. Tom ne bina koi sabd kahe head aur uske kawach par thappadon ki bauchhar kar di (rained cuffs): victim ne har ek blow ko ek binnati karte hue receive kiya, “Please, Marse Tom!—oh, please, Marse Tom!” Saat thappad—phir Tom ne kaha, “Door ki taraf face karo—march!” Unhone ek, do, teen solid kicks (laathon) ke sath piche se follow kiya. Aakhiri laath ne us poore safed gulam (pure-white slave) ko door dehleez ke paar push kiya, aur woh apni purani fate-purane sleeve se apni aankhon ko pochte hue ladkhada kar chala gya. Tom uske peeche chilla uthe, “Use andar bhejo!”

Phir unhone haanfte hue (panting) khud ko dobara sofa par phenk diya, aur tippani nikaali, “Woh theek sahi moment par aaya; main karrwe vicharon se poori tarah upar tak bhara tha, aur badla nikaalne ke liye koi nahi tha. Yeh kitna refreshing tha! Main behtar feel kar raha hoon.”

Tom ki mother ne ab enter kiya, apne piche door close karte hue, aur un saari phuslaane wali aur binnati karti gulamiyat (wheedling and supplicating servilities) ke sath apne bete ke paas aayin jo darr aur interest ek janmjaat gulam ke lafzon aur postures ko pradan kar sakte hain. Woh apne boy se ek yard ki doori par rukin aur uske mardana stature aur general handsomeness par do ya teen adbhut tareefon ke chillane (admiring exclamations) kiye, aur Tom ne properly indifferent (bina parwah ke) dikhne ke liye apna ek haath apne head ke neeche rakkha aur ek leg ko sofa-back ke upar utha liya.

“My lan’, tum kitne badh gaye ho, honey! Sach keh rahi hoon, main tumhein pehchan nahi paati, Marse Tom! Sach mein nahi pehchanti! Mujhe achhi tarah dekho; kya tumhein purani Roxy yaad hai?—kya tum apni purani nigger mammy ko jaante ho, honey? Well, ab, main shanti se let kar mar sakti hoon, kyunki maine seed (dekh liya) hai—”

“Chhota karo ise, d--- it, chhota karo! Tumhein kya chahiye?”

“Aapne suna? Exactly wahi same purane Marse Tom, hamesha ole mammy ke sath itne gay aur funnin’ karne wale. Main bilkul shore thin—”

“Chhota karo ise, main tumhein kehta hoon, aur aige badho! Tumhein kya chahiye?”

Yeh ek karrwi niraasha (bitter disappointment) thi. Roxy ne itne dino tak is dharana ko paala (nourished) aur dulaara tha ki Tom apni purani nurse ko dekh kar glad hoga, aur ek-do saaf lafzon se unhein andar tak proud aur happy karega, ki unhein do baar jhatke (two rebuffs) lene pade yeh convince karne ke liye ki woh mazaak nahi kar raha tha, aur unka khoobsurat dream ek andha aur moorkhta-purna ghamand (fond and foolish vanity) tha, ek ghatiya aur taras-yogya galti thi. Unhein dil par chot pahunchei thi, aur woh itni ashamed thin ki ek moment ke liye woh poori tarah nahi jaanti thin ki kya karein ya kaise act karein. Phir unqi chaati marodne lagi, aansu aa gaye, aur apni is akelapan (forlornness) mein woh apne us doosre dream ko try karne ke liye prerit huin—apne boy ki charity (daan) ke liye ek appeal; aur isliye, ek jhatke mein (impulse), aur bina vichar kiye, unhone apni binnati prastut ki:

“Oh, Marse Tom, poori ole mammy in dino bahut hard luck mein hai; aur haanthon se thodi si crippled hai aur kaam nahi kar sakti, aur agar aap mujhe ek dollar de sakein—sirf ek chota sa dol—”

Tom itni sudden apne pairon par khade ho gaye ki binnati karne wali khud jhatke se jump kar gayi.

“Ek dollar!—tumhein ek dollar doon! Mera dimaag tumhara gala ghhontne (strangle you) ka ho raha hai! Kya yahi tumhara kaam tha yahan? Baahar niklo! Aur jaldi karo is baare mein!”

Roxy slowly door ki taraf piche hatin (backed slowly). Jab woh aadhe raaste thin toh woh ruk gayin, aur udaasi se kehti thin:

“Marse Tom, maine tumhein tab sambhala (nussed) tha jab tum ek chote baby the, aur maine tumhein apne dum par bada kiya jab tak tum lagbhag ek young man nahi ho gaye; aur ab tum young aur rich ho, aur main poor aur boodhi ho rahi hoon, aur main yahan yeh vishwas karke aayi thin ki aap ole mammy ki us chote raaste par madad karenge jo uske aur qabr ke beech bacha hai, aur—”

Tom ko yeh sur (tune) unse pehle aane wale kisi bhi sur se kam pasand aaya, kyunki yeh unke zameer (conscience) mein ek tarah ki goonj jagane laga tha; isliye unhone interrupt kiya aur faisale ke sath kaha, bhale hi bina karrwahat ke, ki woh unqi madad karne ki situation mein nahi the, aur aisa nahi karne wale the.

“Kya aap meri kabhi madad nahi karenge, Marse Tom?”

“Nahi! Ab chalao yahan se aur mujhe mazeed pareshan mat karo.”

Roxy ka head neeche tha, namrata ke ek posture (attitude of humility) mein. Lekin ab unke purane apmaanon ki aag unqi chaati mein bhadak uthi aur tezi se jalne lagi. Unhone apna head slowly upar uthaya, jab tak ki yeh poori tarah upar nahi ho gya, aur same samay par unqi vishal kad-kaathi ne anjaane mein ek seedha aur master-bhara posture (erect and masterful attitude) le liya, jisme unqi khoyi hui youth ki saari majeste aur grace majood thi. Unhone apni ungli uthai aur isse nishana lagaya (punctuated with it):

“Tumne sabd keh diya hai. Tumhe tumhara chance mila tha, aur tumne ise apne pairon ke tehat kuchtal diya hai. Jab tumhein doosra milega, toh tum apne knees par baith kar iske liye bheekh mangoge (beg for it)!”

Tom ke dil mein ek cold chill (thand) chali gayi, woh nahi jaante the kyun; kyunki unhone ispar vichar nahi kiya tha ki aise ek asangat srot (incongruous source) se aaye, aur itne gombhirta se deliver kiye gaye sabd, us asar mein aasaani se fail nahi ho sakte. Halanki, unhone natural cheez ki: unhone chillane aur mazaak ke sath javab diya:

“Tum mujhe ek chance dogi—tum! Shayad main abhi apne knees par baith jaoon! Lekin in case main na baithoon—bas tark ke liye (argument's sake)—kya hone wala hai, prarthna karein?”

“Yeh hone wala hai. Main jitna seedha chal sakti hoon utna seedha tumhare uncle ke paas ja rahi hoon, aur unhein har ek aakhiri cheez batane wali hoon jo main tumhare baare mein jaanti hoon.”

Tom ke cheeks safed pad gaye (blenched), aur unhone ise dekh liya. Pareshan karne wale vichaar unke head ke beech ek doosre ka peeche karne lage. “Yeh kaise jaan sakti hai? Aur phir bhi isne figure out kar liya hoga—woh waisi hi dikhti hai. Mujhe vasiyat wapas mile sirf teen mahine hue hain, aur main pehle se hi dobara gehre karz mein hoon, aur exposure aur destruction se apne aap ko bachane ke liye aasmaan-paatal ek kar raha hoon, is cheez ko chhupane ke ek reasonable saaf show ke sath agar mujhe akele chhod diya jaye, aur ab is shaitan ne kahin na kahin se mujhe figure out kar liya hai. Main hairan hoon ki yeh kitna jaanti hai? Oh, oh, oh, yeh kisi ka dil todne ke liye kafi hai! Lekin mujhe use khush rakhna hoga (humor her)—koi doosra raasta nahi hai.”

Phir unhone ek chalaki-bhari hansi (gay laugh) ka ek kafi kamzor sample viksit kiya aur tareeqe mein ek khokhli khushi (hollow chipperness) laaye, aur kaha:

“Well, well, Roxy dear, tumhare aur mere jaise purane doston ko quarrel (ladna) nahi chahiye. Yeh raha tumhara dollar—na mujhe batao ki tum kya jaanti ho.”

Unhone us saste note (wild-cat bill) ko badhaya; woh jaisi thin waisi hi khadi rahin, aur koi movement nahi ki. Ab unqi baari thi samjhane wali bewakoofi (persuasive foolery) ko tuchh jaanne (scorn) ki, aur unhone ise barbaad nahi kiya. Unhone awaaz aur tareeqe mein ek karrwi draddhta (grim implacability) ke sath kaha, jisne Tom ko lagbhag realize karwaya ki ek purana gulam bhi ten minutes ke liye un apmaanon aur choton ko yaad rakh sakta hai jo haasil kiye gaye tareefon aur flatteries ke badle diye gaye the, aur opportunity milne par unka badla lene ka anand bhi le sakta hai:

“Main kya jaanti hoon? Main tumhein batati hoon main kya jaanti hoon. Main itna jaanti hoon ki us vasiyat ko tukde-tukde (bu'st dat will to flinders) kar sakoon—aur mazeed, dhyan rakhna, mazeed!”

Tom hairat-mein-tha (aghast).

“Mazeed?” unhone kaha. “Tum mazeed kise kehti ho? Mazeed ke liye kahan koi jagah hai?”

Roxy ek mazaak-bhari hansi hansin, aur vyang se kaha, apne head ke ek jhatke ke sath, aur apne haath apni hips par rakh kar—

“Haan!—oh, main sochti hoon! Co'se aap jaan'na chahenge—apne is poor chote purane raddi dollar (rag dollah) ke sath. Aap kya sochte hain main tumhein kyun batane wali hoon?—aapke paas koi paisa nahi hai. Main aapke uncle ko batane ja rahi hoon—aur main ise isi minute karungi bhi—woh mujhe is news ke liye five dollars denge, aur bahut glad hokar denge.”

Unhone tiraskar se (disdainfully) apne aap ko chaaron taraf ghumaya, aur jaane lagin. Tom ek panic (darr) mein the. Unhone unke skirts ko pakad liya, aur unhein wait karne ke liye implored (binnati) kiya. Woh mudin aur oonche tareeqe se kaha—

“Yahan dekho (Look-a-heah), maine tumhein kya bataya tha?”

“Tumne—tumne—mujhe kuch yaad nahi hai. Tumne mujhe kya bataya تھا?”

“Maine tumhein bataya tha ki agle baar jab main tumhein ek chance dungi toh tum apne knees par baith kar iske liye beg karoge.”

Tom ek moment ke liye sunn (stupefied) ho gaye. Woh utsah se haanf (panting) rahe the. Phir unhone kaha:

“Oh, Roxy, tum apne young master se aishi horrible cheez karne ke liye required nahi karogi. Tumhara matlab yeh nahi ho sakta.”

“Main tumhein bahut jaldi jaan'ne dungi ki mera matlab yeh hai ya nahi! Aap mujhe mean naamon se pukaarte hain, aur jab main yahan poor, bekar aur humble hokar aati hoon aap par thukne ke barabar karte hain, aapki tareef karne ke liye ki tum itne fine aur handsome bade hue ho, aur tumhein batane ke liye ki main kaise tumhein sambhalti thi aur tumhari dekh-bhaal karti thin jab tum sick the aur poori duniya mein mere alava tumhari koi mother nahi thi, aur poor ole nigger ko khane ke liye kuch paane ke liye ek dollar dene ke liye beg karti hoon, aur aap mujhe mean naamon se pukaarte hain—naamon se, d--- you! Haan sir, I gives you jes one chance mo' (main tumhein sirf ek aur chance deti hoon), aur woh abhi hai, aur yeh sirf aadhe second ke liye chalta hai—sun rahe ho?”

Tom apne knees par baith gaye (slumped to his knees) aur beg karna shuru kar diya, kehte hue—

“Aap dekh rahi hain, main beg kar raha hoon, aur yeh honest begging hai! Ab mujhe batao, Roxy, mujhe batao.”

Do sau saal ke bina-badle apmaan aur utpeedan (unatoned insult and outrage) ke waaris ne unpar neeche dekha aur aisa laga jaise santusht ke gehre ghhont (deep draughts of satisfaction) pee rahi ho. Phir unhone kaha—

“Fine nice young white gentleman ek nigger-wench ke samne ghutno par baitha hai! Main ise bulaye jaane se pehle (marne se pehle) ek baar dekhna chahti thin. Ab, Gabriel, bhonpu bajao (blow de hawn), main ready hoon … Uth khade ho (Git up)!”

Tom ne aisa kiya. Unhone humby kaha—

“Now, Roxy, mujhe mazeed punish mat karo. Jo mujhe mila main iske layak tha, lekin achhi bano aur mujhe iske sath chhod do. Uncle ke paas mat jao. Mujhe batao—main tumhein five dollars dunga.”

“Haan, main bet lagati hoon aap denge; aur aap wahin rukenge bhi nahi, doosra bhi nahi. Lekin main tumhein yahan nahi batane wali—”

“Good gracious, nahi!”

“Kya aap ha'nted house (bhootiya ghar) se darrte (feard) hain?”

“N-nahi.”

“Well, toh, aap aaj raat das ya gyaarah baje ke aas-paas ha'nted house mein aana, aur ladder (seedhi) par upar climb karna, kyunki stairs ke steps toote hue hain, aur aap mujhe paa lenge. Main ha'nted house mein reh (roostin') rahi hoon kyunki main kahin aur rehna afford nahi kar sakti.” Woh door ki taraf badhi, lekin ruki aur kaha, “Mujhe dollar bill do!” Unhone ise unhein de diya. Unhone ise jaanch (examined) kiya aur kaha, “H'm—lagta hai bank collapse ho gya hai.”* Woh dobara badhi, lekin dobara ruki. “Kya aapke paas koi whisky hai?”

“Haan, thodi si.”

“Lao ise!”

Woh upar apne room ki taraf bhaage aur ek bottle neeche le aaye jo do-tihaai (two-thirds) bhari thi. Unhone ise upar jhukaaya aur ek drink li. Unqi aankhein santushti se sparkled huin, aur unhone bottle ko apne shawl ke neeche dba liya, kehti hui, “Yeh kamaal (prime) hai. Main ise sath le jaungi.”

Tom ne humbly unke liye door hold kiya, aur woh ek grenadier (fauji) ki tarah karrwi aur erect ho kar march karte hue baahar nikal gayin.

---

# Chapter IX — Tom Practises Sycophancy

### *(Tom Chaploosi Ka Abhyas Karta Hai)*

---

> *Why is it that we rejoice at a birth and grieve at a funeral? It is because we are not the person involved.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Aisa kyun hai ki hum janam par khush hote hain aur janaze [funeral] par dukh jatate hain? Yeh isliye hai kyunki hum khud usmein shamil [involved] insaan nahi hote.)*
> *It is easy to find fault, if one has that disposition. There was once a man who, not being able to find any other fault with his coal, complained that there were too many prehistoric toads in it.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Galti nikaalna aasan hai, agar kisi ka mizaaj [disposition] hi aisa ho. Ek baar ek mard tha jo apne bhashan ke koyle [coal] mein koi aur galti nahi dhoondh saka, toh usne shikayat ki ki ismein bahut zyaada pragaitihasik mendhak [prehistoric toads] hain.)*

---

Tom ne khud ko sofa par phenk diya, aur apne teez dhadakte head (throbbing head) ko apne haathon mein le liya, aur apni elbows ko apne knees par tika diya. Woh apne aap ko aage-peeche jhhulane (rocked) laga aur karaahne (moaned) laga.

“Main ek nigger wench ke samne ghutno par baitha hoon!” woh bhurbhuraya. “Maine socha tha ki maine pehle hi apmaan ke sabse gehre andhere (deepest depths of degradation) ko chhua hai, lekin oh, dear, yeh uske samne kuch bhi nahi tha. … Well, ek raahat (consolation) hai, jaisi bhi ho—maine is baar bottom (sabse nichla hissa) chhu liya hai; isse neeche kuch nahi hai.”

Lekin yeh ek jaldi mein nikaala gaya nateejah (hasty conclusion) تھا.

Raat ke das baje woh ha'nted house mein ladder par upar chadha, pale (peela), weak aur wretched (behal) hokar. Roxy ek room ke door par khadi thin, wait karti hui, kyunki unhone use sun liya था.

Yeh ek do-manzil ke lakdi ka ghar (two-story log house) tha jisne kuch saal pehle bhootiya (haunted) hone ki reputation haasil ki thi, aur wahi iski usefulness ka ant tha. Uske baad koi ismein nahi rehta tha, ya raat ko iske paas nahi jata tha, aur zyaada tar log din mein bhi isse door rehte (wide berth) the. Kyunki iska koi competition nahi tha, isliye ise ha'nted house kaha jata tha. Yeh ab lambe neglect ke kaaran jhajhar aur barbaad (crazy and ruinous) ho raha tha. Yeh Pudd’nhead Wilson ke ghar se teen sau yards pare khada tha, beech mein sirf khaali jagah (vacancy) thi. Yeh us end par town ka aakhiri ghar tha.

Tom Roxy ke peeche room mein gaya. Unke paas bed ke roop mein kone mein saaf phoos (clean straw) ka ek dher tha, deewar par kuch saste lekin well-kept kapde latak rahe the, ek tin ki lantern floor par roshni ke chote spots ke sath jhaiyan (freckling) bana rahi thi, aur chaaron taraf sabun aur candle ke tarah-tarah ke boxes bikhre the, jo chairs ka kaam karte the. Dono baith gaye. Roxy ne kaha—

“Ab den, main tumhein seedhe-seedhe batati hoon, aur main paise baad mein ikhatha (k'leck) karna shuru karungi; main kisi hurry mein nahi hoon. Tum kya assume karte ho main tumhein kya batane wali hoon?”

“Well, aap—aap—oh, Roxy, ise mere liye bahut zyaada hard mat banao! Seedhe baahar aao aur mujhe batao ki aapne kisi tarah figure out kar liya hai ki aashiqui aur bewakoofi (dissipation and foolishness) ke kaaran main kis kharab haalat mein hoon.”

“Mizaaj aur bewakoofi (Disposition en foolishness)! No sir, dat ain’t it. Jo main jaanti hoon, uske samne yeh bilkul kuch bhi nahi hai.”

Tom ne unqi taraf ghoora, aur kaha—

“Why, Roxy, aapka matlab kya hai?”

Woh uthi, aur ek Fate (kismat/kaal) ki tarah uske upar andhera (gloomed) ban gayi.

“Mera matlab yeh hai—aur yeh Lord ka sach hai. Tum ole Marse Driscoll ke koi rishte-dar (kin) nahi ho jitni main hoon!—mera yahi matlab hai!” aur unqi aankhein jeet (triumph) se bhadak uthin.

“Kya!”

“Yassir, aur yeh sab kuch nahi hai! Tum ek nigger ho!—ek nigger aur ek gulam paada hue!—aur tum isi minute ek nigger aur ek gulam ho; aur agar maine apna mouf khola toh ole Marse Driscoll tumhein do din mazeed bada hone se pehle hi river ke neeche bech denge!”

“Yeh ek thundering lie (bhaari jhooth) hai, tum badkismat purani blatherskite (bak-bak karne wali)!”

“Yeh koi jhooth nahi hai, dono nahi. Yeh jes sach hai, aur sach ke sivaye kuch nahi, so he'p me. Yassir—you’s my son (tum mere bete ho)—”

“Tum shaitan!”

“Aur woh poor boy jise tum aaj laat aur thappad maar rahe the (a-kickin' en a-cuffin') woh Percy Driscoll ka son hai aur tumhara master—”

“Tum jaanwar!”

“Aur uska naam Tom Driscoll hai, aur tumhara naam Valet de Chambre hai, aur tumhare paas koi fambly name nahi hai, kyunki niggers ke paas woh nahi hote!”

Tom jhatke se utha aur lakdi ka ek danda (billet of wood) pakad kar use upar uthaaya; lekin unqi mother sirf unpar hasin, aur unhone kaha—

“Baith jao (Set down), tum pup (pille)! Kya tum sochte ho tum mujhe darr (skyer) sakte ho? Yeh tumhare andar nahi hai, aur na hi tum jaise logon mein. Main sochti hoon tum mujhe peeth mein goli maar doge, maybe, agar tumhein chance mile, kyunki exactly yahi tumhara style hai—I knows you, throo en throo (main tumhein andar tak jaanti hoon)—lekin main maare jaane par parwah nahi karti, kyunki yeh sab likhit mein (down in writin') hai aur yeh safe hands mein bhi hai, aur jis mard ke paas yeh hai woh jaanta hai ki jab main maari jaoon toh sahi mard ko kahan dhoondhna hai. Oh, bless yo’ soul, agar tum apni mother ko apne jitna bada bewakoof assume karte ho, toh tum pow’ful mistaken ho, main tumhein bata sakti hoon! Ab den, tum shant baitho aur behave karo; aur jab tak main tumhein na kahon dobara mat uthna!”

Tom ek bhramit karne wale ehsaason aur emotions ke toofaan (whirlwind of disorganizing sensations) ke beech thodi der tak chid-chida (fretted and chafed) raha, aur finally nishchit vishwas (settled conviction) jaisi kisi cheez ke sath kaha—

“Yeh poori cheez bamatlab (moonshine) hai; ab den, aige badho aur apna badtar karo; mera aapke sath hisab khatam.”

Roxy ne koi javab nahi diya. Unhone lantern li aur door ki taraf badhin. Tom ek hi moment mein ek cold panic (darr) mein aa gaya.

“Wapas aao, wapas aao!” woh chillaaya. “Mera woh matlab nahi tha, Roxy; main sab kuch wapas leta hoon, aur main ise dobara kabhi nahi kahunga! Please wapas aao, Roxy!”

Aurat ek moment ke liye khadi rahi, phir unhone gombhirta (gravely) se kaha:

“Yeh ek cheez aapko rokni hogi, Valet de Chambers. Tum mujhe Roxy nahi pukaar sakte, theek same jaise ki tum mere barabar ke ho. Chillen apni mammies se is tareeqe se baat nahi karte. Tum mujhe ma ya mammy pukaaroge, exactly yahi tum mujhe pukaaroge—kam se kam jab aas-paas koi na ho. Kaho ise!”

Isne Tom ko ek struggle ki keemat lagai, lekin unhone ise nikaal diya.

“Woh alright hai. Agar tum jaante ho ki tumhare liye kya achha hai toh ise dobara kabhi mat bhoolna. Ab den, tumne kaha hai ki tum ise dobara kabhi lies aur moonshine nahi kahonge. Main tumhein ek warning ke roop mein yeh batati hoon: agar tumne dobara kabhi aisa kaha, toh yeh aakhiri baar hoga jab tum mujhe aisa kahonge; main jitna seedha chal sakti hoon utna seedha Judge ke paas jaungi, aur unhein batayengi tum kaun ho, aur ise prove karungi. Kya tum mera vishwas karte ho jab main aisa kehti hoon?”

“Oh,” Tom karaahya, “main vishwas karne se mazeed karta hoon; ichha ke sath jaanta hoon.”

Roxy jaanti thin unqi jeet complete thi. Woh kisi ke samne kuch bhi prove nahi kar saktin thin, aur likhit saaman ke baare mein unqi threat ek jhooth thi; lekin woh us insaan ko jaanti thin jiske sath woh deal kar rahi thin, aur unhone is asar ke baare mein bina kisi shakk ke dono statements diye the jo unhone produce kiya.

Woh gayin aur apne candle-box par baith gayin, aur unqi jeetne wali position ke garv aur shandari ne ise ek throne (singhasan) bana diya. Unhone kaha—

“Ab den, Chambers, hum business ki baat karne ja rahe hain, aur ab koi mazeed bewakoofi nahi hone wali hai. Pehli jagah par, tumhein fifty dollars a month milte hain; tum iska aadha hissa apni ma ko han' over karne ja rahe ho. Nikalo ise (Plank it out)!”

Lekin Tom ke paas duniya mein sirf khali six dollars the. Unhone unhein woh de diye, aur agle mahine ke pension par sahi shuruat karne ka vaada kiya.

“Chambers, tum kitne karz mein ho?”

Tom kaanp utha, aur unhone kaha—

“Lagbhag teen sau dollars.”

“Tum ise kaise pay karne ja rahe ho?”

Tom ne karaahte hue nikaala—“Oh, main nahi jaanta; mujhse aise awful sawaal mat poochie.”

Lekin woh apne point par tiki rahin jab kaapkar unhone usse ek confession baahar nikaal liya: woh disguise (bhes badal kar) mein chaaron taraf ghoom raha tha, private gharon se choti keemti cheezein chura raha tha; in fact, unhone do hafte pehle apne saathi-villagers par ek achhi khase raid ki thi, jab unhein St. Louis mein hona mana gya tha; lekin unhein shak tha ki unhone required amount haasil karne jitna saaman baahar bheja hai ya nahi, aur town ke majooda excited state mein ek aur venture karne se darr rahe the.

Unqi mother ne unke is vyavahar ko approve kiya, aur madad offer ki, lekin isne unhein darr (frightened) diya. Unhone kaanpte hue yeh kehne ki dharstata ki agar woh town se chali jayein toh woh behtar aur safer feel karenge, aur apne head ko mazeed ooncha hold kar sakenge—aur ek tark dene wale the, lekin unhone interrupt kiya aur unhein pleasantly surprise karte hue kaha ki woh ready hain; unhein koi farq nahi padta tha ki woh kahan rahein, bhasharte unhein pension ka apna hissa regularly milta rahe. Unhone kaha ki woh bahut door nahi jayengi, aur apne paise ke liye mahine mein ek baar ha'nted house mein aayengi. Phir unhone kaha—

“Main ab tumse utni nafrat nahi karti, lekin maine tumse kai saal nafrat ki hai—aur koi bhi karta. Kya maine tumhein badla nahi, aur tumhein ek achhi fambly aur ek achha naam diya, aur tumhein ek white gentleman aur rich banaya, kapdo ke sath—aur mujhe iske badle kya mila? Tum poore samay mujhse ghrina (despised) karte the, aur hamesha logon ke samne mujhe mean hard cheezein kehte the, aur mujhe kabhi bhoolne nahi dete the ki main ek nigger hoon—en—en———”

Woh rone lagin, aur toot gayin. Tom ne kaha—“Lekin aap jaanti hain main nahi jaanta tha ki aap meri mother hain; aur iske alava—”

“Well, parwah nahi us baare mein ab; ise jaane do. Main ise bhoolne ja rahi hoon.” Phir unhone tivrata (fierce) se add kiya, “Aur mujhe dobara kabhi ise yaad rakhne par majboor mat karna, ya tum pachtaoge, main tumhein batati hoon.”

Jab woh alag ho rahe the, Tom ne sabse persuasive (samjhane wale) tareeqe se kaha jise woh command kar sakte the—

“Ma, kya aap mujhe batane mein parwah karengi ki mere father kaun the?”

Unhone assume kiya tha ki woh ek embarrassing sawaal pooch rahe hain. Woh galat the. Roxy apne head ke ek garv-bhare jhatke ke sath seedhi khadi huin, aur unhone kaha—

“Kya mujhe batane mein parwah hai? No, dat I don’t! Tumhare paas apne father par ashamed hone ka koi kaaran (casion) nahi hai, main tumhein bata sakti hoon. Woh is poore town mein sabse oonche quality (highest class) ke the—ole Virginny stock. First famblies ke the. Exactly utna hi achha stock jitna Driscolls aur Howards ka hai, sabse behtar din jo unhone kabhi dekha ho.” Unhone agar possible ho toh thoda mazeed proud air pehan liya, aur impressively add kiya: “Kya tumhein Cunnel Cecil Burleigh Essex yaad hain, jo usi saal mare the jis saal tumhare young Marse Tom Driscoll ke pappy mare the, aur saare Masons aur Odd Fellows aur Churches baahar aaye the aur unhein is town ka sabse bada janaza (bigges' funeral) diya tha? Wahi mard hain.”

Unqi badhti hui santushti (soaring complacency) ke inspiration ke tehat unqi youth ke departs hue graces unke paas wapas laut aaye, aur unke tareeqe ne apne andar ek aishi dignity aur state le li jo rani jaisi (queenly) maani ja sakti thi agar unka aas-paas ka environment iske sath thoda mazeed mel khata hota.

“Is town mein aisa koi doosra nigger nahi hai jo tumhare jitna high-bawn (oonche khandaan ka) ho. Ab den, chalao aige! Aur bas tum apna head jitna ooncha chaaho utna hold karke rakkho—tumhare paas adhikaar hai, aur iski main kasam (swah) kha sakti hoon.”

---

# Chapter X — The Nymph Revealed

### *(Sundari Ka Khulasa)*

---

> *All say, “How hard it is that we have to die”—a strange complaint to come from the mouths of people who have had to live.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Sabhi kehte hain, “Marna kitna kathin hai”—ek ajeeb shikayat hai un logon ke mouf se aana jinhone zindagi ko jeeya hai.)*
> *When angry, count four; when very angry, swear.—Pudd’nhead Wilson’s Calendar.*
> *(Jab gussa aaye, toh chaar tak ginte; jab bahut zyaada gussa aaye, toh gaali dete.)*

---

Har kuch samay baad, Tom ke bed par jaane ke baad, unqi neend se sudden jhatke se jaag khul jaati thin, aur unka pehla vichaar hota, “Oh, khushi (joy), yeh sab ek dream tha!” Phir woh ek karaah (groan) aur bhurbhuraye lafzon ke sath dobara bhaari roop se let jaate, “Ek nigger! Main ek nigger hoon! Oh, kaash main mar gya hota!”

Woh bhor (dawn) ke samay is horror ke ek aur dohraav (repetition) ke sath jaage, aur tab unhone nishchay kiya ki woh us dhokebaaz neend (treacherous sleep) ke sath mazeed koi her-pher (meddle) nahi karenge. Woh sochne lage.

Woh kaafi karrwe vichaar (bitter thinkings) the. Woh kuch is dhang se bhatakte rahe:

“Niggers aur whites banaye hi kyun gaye? Us bina-paada hue pehle nigger (uncreated first nigger) ne aisa kya crime kiya tha ki uske liye birth ka shraap (curse) decree kiya gya? Aur white aur black ke beech yeh awful farq kyun banaya gya hai? … Ek nigger ki kismat (fate) aaj subah kitni hard lagti hai!—phir bhi pichli raat tak aisa vichaar mere head mein kabhi enter nahi hua tha.”

Unhone ek ghante ya usse zyaada samay aah bharkar aur karaahte hue bitaya. Phir “Chambers” humby andar aaya yeh kehne ke liye ki breakfast lagbhag taiyar hai. “Tom” yeh dekhkar sharm se laal (blushed scarlet) ho gya ki yeh kulin white youth (aristocratic white youth) uske samne cringed (gulamiyat se jhukna) kar raha hai, ek nigger ke samne, aur use “Young Marster” pukaar raha hai. Unhone roughly kaha—

“Meri nazar se door ho jao (Get out of my sight)!” aur jab youth chala gya, toh woh bhurbhuraye, “Usne mera koi nuksaan (harm) nahi kiya hai, poor wretch, lekin woh ab mere liye ek ankhon ka kaanta (eyesore) hai, kyunki woh Driscoll young gentleman hai, aur main ek—oh, kaash main mar gya hota!”

Ek vishal ubaal (gigantic irruption), jaise kuch saal pehle Krakatoa ka hua tha, uske sath aaye earthquakes, jwalamukhi dhool ke badlon (clouds of volcanic dust) aur tsunami ke sath, aas-paas ke jameen ke nazaare (landscape) ka face pehchan se pare badal deta hai, oonchi jameen ko neeche laata hai, neeche wali ko uthata hai, jahan deserts the wahan sundar lakes banata hai, aur jahan pehle hari prairies muskura rahi thin wahan deserts bana deta hai. Tom par jo vishal aafat (tremendous catastrophe) aayi thi, usne uske naitik nazaare (moral landscape) ko theek usi tareeqe se badal diya tha. Usne paaya ki uske kuch nichle sthan (low places) uth kar ideals ban gaye hain, uske kuch ideals ghaatiyon (valleys) mein doob gaye hain, aur unke tabaah hue heads par pumice-stone aur sulphur ki raakh aur taat (sackcloth and ashes) paada hai.

Saalon tak woh akeli jagahon (lonely places) mein bhatakta raha, sochta, sochta, sochta hua—apna rasta (bearings) paa rahe the. Yeh naya kaam tha. Agar woh kisi dost se milta, toh woh paata ki ek poori life ki habit kisi rahasyamai tareeqe se vanished ho gayi hai—unka haath shake karne ke liye anjaane mein aige badhne ke bajaye limp (dheela) latak jata tha. Yeh unke andar ka “nigger” tha jo apni vinamrata (humility) ko assert kar raha tha, aur woh sharminda aur abashed (lajjit) ho jata. Aur unke andar ka “nigger” hairan hota jab white friend shake karne ke liye apna haath aige badhata. Unhone paaya ki unke andar ka “nigger” sidewalk par anjaane mein ek white rowdy aur loafer (gunde-lafange) ko rasta de deta tha. Jab Rowena, jo unke dil ke liye sabse pyaari cheez thin, unqi gupt pooja ka idol (idol of his secret worship), unhein andar invite karti, toh unke andar ka “nigger” ek jhijhak-bhara bahana (embarrassed excuse) bana deta aur daravne white logon (dread white folks) ke sath barabar ke niyam (equal terms) par enter karne aur baithne se darta tha. Unke andar ka “nigger” yahan-wahan aur har taraf सिकुड़ता aur chhupta (shrinking and skulking) phirta, aur kalpana karta ki use saarre faces, tones, aur gestures mein shak aur maybe pehchan (suspicion and maybe detection) dikh rahi hai.

Tom ka vyavahar itna ajeeb aur aswabhavik (uncharacteristic) tha ki logon ne ise notice kiya, aur jab woh aige badh jata toh unke peeche mud kar dekhte; aur jab woh peeche glance karta—jaisa woh apni sabse behtar resistance ke bavajood karne se khud ko rok nahi sakta tha—aur kisi ke face par us hairani ke expression (puzzled expression) ko pakadta, toh yeh use ek bimar ehsaas (sick feeling) de deta, aur woh jitna jaldi ho sake khud ko nazar se door kar leta. Jaldi hi unke paas ek shikar kiye hue insaan ka ehsaas (hunted sense) aur ek hunted look aa gaya, aur phir woh pahadiyon ke peaks (hill-tops) aur akelepan (solitudes) ki taraf bhaag gya. Unhone apne aap se kaha ki unpar Ham ka shraap (curse of Ham) paada hai.

Unhon apne khane-peene (meals) se darr lagta tha; unke andar ka “nigger” white logon ki table par baithne mein sharminda hota tha, aur poore samay discovery (khulase) se darta tha; aur ek baar jab Judge Driscoll ne kaha, “Tumhein kya mamla hai? Tum ek nigger jitne namra (meek as a nigger) dikhte ho,” toh unhone waisa feel kiya jaisa kaha jata hai ki gupt khuni (secret murderers) feel karte hain jab aarop lagane wala kehta hai, “Tum hi woh mard ho (Thou art the man)!” Tom ne kaha ki unqi health theek nahi hai, aur table chhod di. Unqi dikhne wali “aunt” ki chintayein (solicitudes) aur dulaar ab unke liye ek terror ban chuke the, aur woh unse bachte the. Aur poore samay, unke dikhne wai “uncle” ke khilaf nafrat unke dil mein steadily badh rahi thi; kyunki unhone apne aap se kaha, “Woh white hai; aur main uska saaman (chattel) hoon, uski property, uska maal, aur woh mujhe bech sakta hai, exactly jaise woh apne dog ko bech sakta tha.”

Iske baad lagbhag ek hafte tak, Tom ne kalpana ki ki unke charitra (character) mein ek kaafi bada badlav (radical change) aaya hai. Lekin aisa isliye tha kyunki woh khud ko nahi jaante the. Kai tareeqon se unke opinions poori tarah badal gaye the, aur kabhi wapas nahi jayenge jo woh pehle the, lekin unke charitra ka mukhya dhancha (main structure) badla nahi tha, aur badla nahi ja sakta tha. Iske ek-do bahut important features badal gaye the, aur samay ke sath isse effects nikalte, agar opportunity milti toh—kaafi serious nature ke effects dono. Ek bade dimaagi aur naitik upheavel (mental and moral upheaval) ke influence ke tehat unke charitra aur habits ne poore badlav ka appearance le liya tha, lekin thodi der baad toofaan ke shant hone (subsidence of the storm) ke sath dono apne purane sthanon ki taraf baithna (settle) shuru ho gaye. Woh gradually wapas apne purane frivolous (halke) aur easy-going tareeqon aur ehsaason ki conditions aur bolne ke tareeqe mein slip ho gaye, aur unka koi bhi parichit (familiar) unmein aishi koi cheez detect nahi kar sakta tha jo unhein pichele dino ke weak aur laparwah Tom se alag (differentiate) karti ho.

Unhone village par jo chori ki raid (theft-raid) ki thi, uska nateejah usse kahin behtar nikla jitni unhone umeed karne ki dharstata ki thi. Isne unke juye ke karz ko pay karne ke liye required amount produce kiya, aur unhein unke uncle ke samne expose hone aur vasiyat ke ek aur smash hone se bacha liya. Woh aur unqi mother ek doosre ko kaafi achhi tarah pasand karna seekh gaye the. Woh abhi unse pyaar nahi kar saktin thin, kyunki "usmein kuch dam nahi tha (warn't nothing to him)," jaisa unhone express kiya, lekin unqi nature ko raj karne ke liye (rule over) kisi cheez ya kisi insaan ki zarurat thi, aur woh kuch na hone se behtar tha. Unke strong character aur aakramak aur aadesh-shahi tareeqon (aggressive and commanding ways) ne Tom ke admiration ko majboor kiya is fact ke bavajood ki unhein unke comfort ke hisab se zarurat se zyaada iske examples mile. Halanki, ek rule ke roop mein unqi baatcheet town ke mukhya families ki privacies ke baare mein chalu gappe (racy tattle) thin (kyunki jab bhi woh village aatin toh unke kitchens ke beech harvesting kartin thin), aur Tom ne iska anand liya. Yeh exactly unqi line mein tha. Woh hamesha punctually (samay par) apna pension ka aadha hissa ikhatha kartin, aur Tom in mauqon par unse chat karne ke liye hamesha ha'nted house mein rehte the. Kabhi-kabar woh beech ke dino mein bhi wahan unqi visit kartin thin.

Occasionally woh kuch hafton ke liye St. Louis bhaag jaate, aur aakhirkar temptation (laalach) ne unhein dobara pakad liya. Unhone dheron paise jeete, lekin unhein haar gaye, aur iske sath hi ek bada hissa mazeed bhi, jise unhone jitna jaldi possible ho raise karne ka vaada kiya. Is maqsad ke liye unhone apne town par ek nayi raid plan (projected) ki. Woh kabhi kisi doosre town ke sath her-pher nahi karte the, kyunki woh aise gharon mein venture karne se darte the jinke andar-baahar (ins and outs) ko woh nahi jaante the aur jinki households ki habits se woh parichit nahi the. Woh twins ke aane se pehle Wednesday ko disguise (bhes badal kar) ha'nted house pahunche—apni aunt Pratt ko yeh likhne ke baad ki woh do din baad tak arrive nahi honge—aur Friday subah bhor hone tak apni mother ke sath wahin hiding mein rahe, jab woh apne uncle ke ghar gaye aur apni khud ki key ke sath piche ke raaste se enter hue, aur apne room mein slip ho gaye, jahan woh mirror aur toilet articles ka use kar sakte the. Unhone apni raid ke liye disguise ke roop mein ek bundle mein girl’s clothes ka ek suit apne sath rakkha tha, aur apni mother ke kapdo ka ek suit pehne hue the, black gloves aur veil ke sath. Bhor hone tak woh apni raid ke liye taiyar (tricked out) the, lekin unhone sarak ke us paar khidki se Pudd’nhead Wilson ki ek jhalak pakadi, aur jaante the ki Pudd’nhead ne unqi ek jhalak pakad li hai.

Isliye unhone thodi der tak Wilson ko kuch shandariyon aur postures ke sath entertain kiya, phir nazar se door hat gaye aur doosra disguise dobara le liya, aur gradually piche ke raaste se neeche aur baahar nikal gaye aur apne intended labors (chori ke kaam) ke scene ka nirdesh nikaalne (reconnoiter) ke liye down town chal pade. Lekin woh ashant (ill at ease) the. Woh wapas Roxy ki dress par badal gaye the, disguise mein umra ka jhukaav (stoop of age) add karke, taaki agar Wilson abhi bhi jasoosi (spying) kar raha ho toh woh jaldi subah piche ke raaste se neighbor ke ghar se nikalne wali ek mamuli purani aurat ke baare mein khud ko pareshan na karein. Lekin assume karein Wilson ne unhein nikalte hue dekh liya ho, aur ise suspicious socha ho, aur unka peeche bhi kiya ho? Us vichaar ne Tom ko cold kar diya. Unhone din ke liye raid chhod di, aur apne jaan'ne wale sabse gupt raaste (obscurest route) se ha'nted house ki taraf jaldi ki.

Unqi mother chali gayi thin; lekin woh thodi der mein wapas aayin, Patsy Cooper ke yahan shandaar reception ki news lekar, aur jaldi hi unhein convince kiya ki yeh opportunity ek khas kripa (special providence) ki tarah hai, yeh itna inviting aur perfect tha.
